002 **, ,BI L'A LI T'A BH'U MI DZA GA SYA N'A THA;, DRI Bm'A NA

**, ,RNAM PAR ROL PA SA GSUM 'GRO BA'I MGON,,GSUM LDAN RDO RJE 'DZIN
PA'I ZHABS LA 'DUD,

SANGS RGYAS KUN LAS SNGAR SANGS RGYAS KYANG SANGS RGYAS SRAS KYI
RNAM PA 'DZIN, ,SRID PAR SKYE BA YONGS SU ZAD KYANG SRID PAR
SKYE BA'I TSUL YANG STON, ,SEMS CAN 'GA' YANG GZIGS PA MED KYANG

SEMS CAN DON LA RTAG GZHOL BA, ,SMRA BA ZLA MED 'JAM PA'I
BYANGS KYIS SMRA BA MCHOG GI DNGOS GRUB STZOL, ,DBANG GZHU'I
LDING KHANG DBUS NA CHU SKYES GDAN STENG CHAGS PA'I NYAMS KYIS TZOG

BUR BZHUGS, ,MNYEN LCUGS SOR MOS BSKUL BA'I RGYUD STON DBYANGS KYIS
SNYAN TSIG MI ZAD 'DOD PA 'JO, MTSAR SDUG LANG TSO'I DPAL LA
RGYAL BA RNAMS KYANG RJES CHAGS SPYAN GYIS RTAG TU

GZIGS, ,DBYANGS CAN NGANG PA'I BU MO BDAG SNYING PAD MTSOR DUS
KUN DGYES PAS RTZEN PAR MDZOD, ,YE SHES ME LONG GTZANG MAR SHES
BYA'I RI MO MTHA' DAG RDZOGS PAR BKRA, ,LEGS

BSHAD GRU CHAR GYO BAS BSHAD SGRUB BSTAN PA'I CHU GTER RGYAS PAR
MDZAD, ,'PHRIN LAS NYI ZLA'I SGRON MES 'JIG RTAN RGUD PA'I MUN
PA KUN SEL BA, ,DPAL LDAN BLA MA RIGS BRGYA'I KHYAB

BDAG ROL PA'I RDO RJE RGYAL GYUR CIG ,MI SHIGS RLUNG GI RNAM
'PHRUL RDO RJE'I SKUN NI RNAM PA MED KYANG MTSAN DPE'I RNAM PA
YONGS SU RDZOGS, ,GZHOM MED AA YI RANG GDANGS RDO RJE'I GSUNG NI
RGYUN    

003 **, ,MI 'CHAD KYANG 'BYUNG DANG 'JUG PA'I RTZOL BA BRAL, ,RTOG 
MED BDE CHEN YE SHES RDO RJE'I THUGS NI SPROS DANG BRAL YANG SHES BYA'I
DKYIL 'KHOR KUN LA KHYAB,,

NGOM TSAR YON TAN PHUNG PO KHYAB BDAG RDO RJE'I SEMS KHYOD BDAG SNYING 
'DAB BRGYA'I ZE'U 'BRUR RTAG TU BZHUGS, ,SGRIB BRAL CHOS SKU'I NAM MKHAR
MKHYEN BZANG NYI ZLA ZUNG GIS RTZEN PAS DNGOS

DANG DNGOS MED RANG BZHING GSAL BAR MDZAD, ,DGRA GNYIN BAR MA'I 'GRO LA
NYE RING MI MNGA' BU LTAR BRTZE BAS RTAG TU GZHAN DON 'BA' ZHIG SGRUB LA 
GZHOL, ,YID SRUBS SDE BCAS GTAN  

DU 'JOMS PA'I NUS PA YONGS RDZOGS DPAG BSAM SHING LTAR SKYES RGU'I
SKONG 'PHRIN LAS MNGA', ,GANG GI YON TAN SA DANG RGYA MTSO'I RDOL
GRANGS JI BZHIN DPAG PAR DKA' ZHING BRDZOD PA'I YUL

LAS RAB TU 'DAS, ,CHOS KYI DBYINGS DANG NAM MKHA' JI TZAM PA, ,GANG
GI SKU GSUNG THUGS KYANG DE TZAM STE, ,JI TZAM LAS DANG NYON MONGS  
SEMS CAN MTHA', ,GANG GI 'PHRIN LAS MTHA' YANG

DE TZAM MO, ,'DI NA KA LAN TA KA'I GSHOG RLABS RTZAL GYIS NAM MKHA'I PHA 
MTHA' 'TSOL BA'I NGAL BA LHUR LEN DANG, ,BYIS PA 'GA' YIS GTING ZAB
CHU GTER CHEN PO AA MRA'I TSIG GUS BCUS

TE ZAD PAR RE BA BZHIN, ,RGYAL SRAS THOS SGROG BSE RU'I TSOGS KYI BLO 
GROS RA BA LAS 'GONG BLA MA'I YON TAN LHUN PO NI, ,'CHING BA KUN LDAN
TSUR MTHONG BDAG 'DRA'I BLO GROS CHUNG NGU'I KHAB KYI MIG BUR JI LTAR          

TSUD PAR NUS, ,'ON KYANG MYA NGAM THANG DU SKOM PA YIS, ,GDUNGS PA'I 
SKYE BOS CHU KLUNG RNYED PA NA, ,RDZOGS PAR BTUNG MA NUS KYANG CHA TZAM
ZHIG  ,SPYAD PA YIS KYANG GDUNG BA SEL BAR 'GYUR, ,DE BZHIN DGE 

BA'I BSHES KYI YON TAN  GYI, ,CHA SHAS TZAM ZHIG GTAM DU BRJOD PAS KYANG, 
,SKAL BZANG SNYING LA 'DOD PA KUN 'JO ZHING, ,BSOD NAMS PHUNG PO MTHA'
YAS SDUD PA NYID, ,DE PHYIR BDAG NI TSE RABS GZHAN

DU YANG, ,MA DAD RNYOG PA BRAL BA'I YID KYI RDZING, ,BLA MA'I YON TAN
'DAB BRGYA'I DPAL 'DZIN PA'I, ,DGE MTSAN NAM YANG NYAMS PAR MA GYUR CES,
,RANG DON LA GUS BSER BUS YANG DANG YANG, ,YID

KYI MA LA YA TSAL BSKYOD PA LAS, ,SKAL BZANG SNYING LA SIM PA MCHOG STER
BA'I, ,RTOGS BRJOD BSUNG ZHIM 'THUL BA KHEGS MA GYUR, ,'DI NA GSER 'OD GLOG
PHRENG DO SHAL CAN, ,SPRIN SNGON MDZES MAS

DBYAR  RNGA BRDUNGS PA NA, ,RMA  BYA GZHON NU NAGS KYI LDING KHANG DU,
,RAB DGA'I ZLOS GAR CI YANG RTZE BA BZHIN, ,BDAG NYID CHEN PO'I KUN
BZANG SPYOD PA'I GTAM, ,SNYAN 'JEBS NGAG GIS DAL BUS GLENG  

004A**, ,PA LA, ,GZUR GNAS TSOGS RNAMS DGA' BA'I 'DZUM DANG BCAS, ,RNA
BA BLGAS TE RTZE GCIG YID KYIS NYON, ,JI SKAD DU, ,SLOB DPON DPA' BOS
MDZAD PA'I BCOM 

LDAN 'DAS KYI SKYIS PA'I RABS LAS, ,GRAS PA'I MTSAN MAR GYUR BA BZANG PO 
'DI RNAMS KYIS, ,BDE BAR GSHES GYUR LAM RNAMS GANG YIN BSTAN PAR 'GYUR,
,YID LA DAD PA MED PA RNAMS KYANG 

DAD PAR 'GYUR, ,CHOS DANG LDAN PA'I GTAM GYIS RAB TU DGA' BAR 'GYUR, 
ZHES DAM PA'I RNAM PAR THAR PA LA BRTEN NAS SKAL BA DANG LDAN PA'I
GDUL BYA RNAM DPYOD CAN DAG GIS SKYIS BU DAM PA RNAMS

GO 'PHANG MTHON POR GSHES PA'I LAM GANG YIN PA SHES NAS PHYIN CI
MA LOG PA'I LAM LA 'JUG PA DANG, DKON MCHOG SGRON ME'I GZUNGS
LAS, DAD PA SNGON 'GRO MA LTAR BSKYED PA STE, ,YON TAN

THAMS CAD BSRUNG ZHIN 'PHEL BAR BYED, ,DOGS PA SEL ZHING CHU RNAMS LAS SGROL, 
,DAD PA BDE LEGS GRONG KHYER MTSON BYED YIN, ,DAD PA RNYOG PA MED CING   
SEMS DANG BYED, ,NGA RGYAL SPONG ZHIN

GUS PA'I RTZA BA YIN, ,DAD PA NOR DANG GTER DANG RKANG PA'I MCHOG
,LAG PA BZHIN DU DGE SNGUD RTZA BA YIN, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR, 
LEGS TSOGS THAMS CAD KYI RTZA BA DAD PA SNGAR MA SKYES PA ZHIN,

SKYES ZIN GONG 'PHEL DU 'GYUR BA DANG, ,CHOS DANG MTHUN PA'I
MRJAD SPYOD BZANG PO RNAMS LA RJES SU YI RANG BAS RANG NYID DAM
PA'I RJES SU SLOB PAR BYED PA SOGS KYI DGOS PA KHYAD PAR CAN DU
MA 'GRUB CING, SMBHU t'I RGYUD LAS,

GANG PHYIR PHYOGS BCU'I SANGS RGYAS DANG, ,BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'I
BSOD NAMS PAS, ,SLOB DPON BA SPU'I KHUNG GCIG MCHOG ,DE PHYIR
SLO DPON MCHOD BYED PA, ,SANGS RGYAS BYANG CHUB SEMS DPAS GZIGS,
,ZHES SOGS MDO 

RGYUD DU MA LAS PHYOGS BCU'I SANGS RGYAS DANG BYANG CHUB SEMS
DPA' THAMS CAD MCHOD PA LAS RANG GI RDO RJE SLOB DPON GYI BA
SPU'I KHUNG BU GCIG MCHOD PA BSOD NAMS CHE BAR GSUNGS PA'I RIGS
PAS SANGS RGYAS DANG BYANG CHUB SEMS 

DPA' THAMS CAD KYI YON TAN BRJOD PA LAS KYANG, BLA MA'I BA SPU'I
KHUNG BU GCIG TZAM GYI BSNGAG PA BRJOD PA BSOD NAMS CHE BAR 'GRUB
PAS, RDO RJE 'CHANG TSAR PA CHOS RJES, GANG DAG RGYA MTSO'I GOS CAN 
RDUL SNYED KYI, ,RGYAL PA

RGYA MTSO'I RMAD BYUNG NGO MTSAR GTAM, ,SRID MTHA'I BAR DU DBYANGS 
SU BSGRAGS PA BAS, ,'DI NA MTSAN LDAN RDO RJE SLOB DPON GYI, ,YON TAN
RTOGS PA BSOD PA'I SHAS TZAM, ,BRJOD B'ANG BSOD NAMS BLA NA MED DO 
ZHES, ,BSLU

MED DAM PA'I GTAM GYIS YID DRANGS NAS, ,BDAG GI YID NI TSUL 'DIR ZHUGS 
PAR GYUR, ,CES GSUNGS SO, ,RGYU MTSAN DE BAS BDAG CAG RNAMS KYI 'DREN 
MCHOG DAM PA, DUS GSUM RGYAL BA MA LUS PA'I MKHYEN BRTZE

005 **, ,GCIG TU BSNGUS PA'I NGO BO, SHES BYA'I DKYIL 'KHOR
MTHA' DAG LA LKOG TU MA GYUR PA'I YE SHES KYI SPYAN DRI MA MED
PA DANG LDAN PA, RANG DANG GZHAN GYI GRUB PA'I MTHA' RGYA MTSO
LTA BU'I PHA ROL

TU SO NA TE  RIG PA'I GNAS MTHA' DAG 'CHAD PA DANG, RTZOD PA
DANG, RTZOM PA LA SA'I STENG 'GRAN PA'I ZLA THAMS CAD DANG BRAL
BA'I SMRA BA'I KHYU MCHOG CHEN PO, RGYAL BA GNYIS PA'I RING
LUGS KYI GDUGS DKAR PO RGYA MTSO'I GOS CAN

GYI KHYON KUN KHYAB PAR 'DEGS PA LA THUGS RJE DANG SNYING STOBS
PHUL DU BYUNG BA, BDE BAR GSHES PA'I GSUNG RAB RAB 'BYAMS KYI DGONGS
PA RANG DBANG DU 'GREL BA LA RNAM DPYOD THOGS PA MED PA'I NGES
PA DON GYI SHING RDAN CHEN PO,

NOR 'RDZIN GYI DKYIL LA 'KHOR LA STOBS KYI 'KHOR LOS SGYUR BA'I
GNAM BSKOS GONG MA CHEN PO LA SOGS PA'I 'DZAM GLING DRIGS LDAN MTHA'
DAG GI GTZUG GI NOR BUS GANG GI ZHABS STEGS KYI PAD MA MNGON PAR
MCHOD PA'I LHA MI'I GTZUG

RGYAN DAM PA, GONG MA BDAG PO CHEN PO'I BKA'I LUNG GIS BKVAN
TING PHU'U SHAN BKANG TSI T'A KOO SHR'AI STE BOD KYI SKAD DU
BYAMS BRTZAS KUN GYI SPYI BO NAS DBANG BSKUR BA'I KUN MKHYEN
CHEN PO ZHES PA'I MTSAN DANG LUNG LAS KYIS MNGON PAR MTHO

BA, RIGS  DANG DKYIL LA 'KHOR KUN GYI KHYAB BDAG DON GYI SLAD DU
MTSAN NAS SMOS TE YONGS RDZOGS BSTAN PA'I MNGA' BDAG THAMS CAD
MKHYEN PA YE SHES BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME ZHES GRAS KYI BA DAN DKAR
POS GSUM NA RNAM PAR GYO BA

DE NYID KYI RNAM PAR THAR PA RGYA MTSO LHA BU LAS SKRA RTZES
BLANGS PA'I THIGS PA TZAM ZHIG RANG GZHAN GYI DAD PA'I GSOS SU
BRJOD PAR BYA'O, ,BDE GSHES GRONG DU BGROD PAR CHAS RNAMS LA,
,RGYAL BA KHYU MCHOG GSHES PA'I LAM 'DI ZHES,,

DRANG POR GSEL BAR STON PA'I SA MKHAN NI, ,RMAD BYUNG DAM PA'I
RNAM PAR THAR PA YIN, ,DE PHYIR RGYAL DANG SRAS NYAN RANG DANG,
,'PHAGS BOD MKHAS GRUB DU MA'I RNAM THAR GYI, ,RIN CHEN PHRENG
BA TSAR DU DNGAR BA YIS, ,THUB BSTAN GSER

GYI BCHOD SDONG MRDZES PAR BYAS, ,MKHAS BTZUN BZANG PO'I RNAM
THAR NYIN BYED KYIS, ,RING NAS BTANG BA SNYIGS MA'I MTSAN DUS
'DIR, ,BSTAN 'GRO'I PHAN NGA DE'I NOR 'BRU CHUD GZON PA'I, ,BYI
BA RKUN PO'I RNAM THAR 'DZIN PA MANG, ,GANG ZHIG

'DI NA CHER RLOM DU MA'I LO RGYUS SRIN BU'I RJES KYIS SA GZHI
BKANG NA YANG, ,STABS LEGS DBANG GIS SRID MTHA' TZAM DU LEGS
SPYAD YI GE'I GZUGS SU GRUB PA NYI TSE LAS, ,PHAL CHER SRID
PA'I RDUL KHROD GYI NAR 'KHYAMS PA'I SPYOD TSUL

GYA GYU'I RI MO 'BA' ZHIG STE, ,GLEGS BAM CHE YANG BON PO'I RNGA
BZHIN GZUGS YOR TZAM LAS SNYING POS STONG PA DES CI BYA, ,TSANGS
SRAS DPAL MOS LHO PHYOGS CHU GTER YONGS SPANGS GANG GI BLO
MTSO'I DBUS NA BDER ROL BA'I, ,NGANG TSUL

DGE BA PHYOGS KYI MDZA' BOR RTOG PAR BYED LA SPRO BA RAB RGYAS
GOM 'GROS CAN, ,NYAMS MED BSOD NAMS 'DZUM DKAR RNAM PAR BKRA
BA'I MRDZES SGEG TSIG PHRENG DO SHAL SKYES THOGS PA'I, ,DAM PA'I
SPYOD TSUL STON PA'I LEGS BSHAD

006 **, ,MCHOG 'DI 'GRO LA DGE LEGS THOG MA'I PHO NYA YIN, ,AA HO
SNYIGS MA BA TSVA'I KHRON PA NAS, ,PHAN BDE'I GZI BYIN 'ONG DU
'BAR BA YI, ,RNAM THAR 'DOD RGU STZOL BA'I NOR RNYID PA, ,

CHOS GYI RDO RJE KHO BO SKAL BA BZANG, ,KVA YE RNAM GROL DON

BU'I

GTZUG RGYAN LONGS, ,DE LTAR THOG MAR DGOS 'BREL CUNG ZAD BRJOD

SKU TSE 'DI

STOGS PA BRJOD PA'O, ,DANG PO NI, JI SKAD DU PHAL PO CHE'I MDO
LAS, BYANG CHUB RGYA MTSO RAB BSNYES GYUR NAS KYANG, ,SEMS CAN
RGYA MTSO RAB TU SMIN BYA'I PHYIR, ,BYANG CHUB SEMS BSKYED RGYA
MTSO STON MDZAD CING, ,MI 'GRIB

SPYOD PA RGYA MTSO DUS KUN STON, ,BDE GSHES RNAMS KYI RNAM
'PHRUL DE 'DRA'O, ,ZHES RDZOGS SMIN SPYANGS GSUM MTHAR PHYIN TE
BLA NA MED PA'I BYANG CHUB MNGON DU MDZAD PA'I SANGS RGYAS BTZOM
LDAN 'DAS RNAMS NI CHOS KYI SKU LAS

GYO BA MED BZHIN DU THUGS RJE CHEN PO'I GZHAN DBANG GIS MDAG
PA'I ZHING DU SEMS CAN GYI DON DU SPRUL PA'I SKU'I MDZAD PA SNA
TSOGS PA NAM MKHA' 'JI SRID GNAS KYI BAR DU STON PAR MDZAD DE,
RGYUD BLA MA LAS, THUGS RJE CHEN POS

'JIG RTAN MKHYEN, ,'JIG RTAN KUN LA GZIGS NAS NI, ,CHOS KYI LAS
MA GYOS PAR, ,SPRUL PA'I RANG BZHIN SNA TSOGS KYIS, ,SKYE BA
MNGON PAR SKYE BA DANG, ,ZHES PA NAS, YONGS SUM DAG ZHING RNAMS
SU, ,SRID PA JI SRID  GNAS PAR STON,,

ZHES GSUNGS, DER MA ZAD SEMS CAN GANG LA GANG 'DUL GYI THABS LA
MKHAS PAS, MKHAS GRUB KYI SKYES BU DANG, RGYAL BLON 'BANGS GSUM,
KHYIM PA PHO MO, THAN BYA DANG RI DVAGS YAN CHAD KYI SEMS LDAN
DANG GRU ZAM GNAS MAL ZAS GOS SA

CHU ME RLUNG SOGS SEMS MED KYI BEM PO'I RNA PA CI RIGS PAS, GDUL
BYA MTHA' DAG GNAS SKABS DANG MTHAR THUG GI PHAN BDE LA 'GONG
PAR MDZAD DE, SDONG PO BKOD PA'I MDO LAS, DE DAG KUN TU 'TSO
BA'I CHOS 'DZIN CING, ,BLA NA YOD DANG

BLA NA MED RNAMS DANG, ,RAL PA RING DANG GZHON NU'I BSTUL ZHUGS
CAN, ,DE DAG GI YANG SLOB DPON 'BYUNG BA YIN, ,DE DAG DGON PAR
LJON SHING CHEN POR 'GYUR, ,SMAN DANG RIN CEN MI ZAD GTER RNAMS
DANG, ,YID BZHIN NOR BU 'DOD PA 'BYIN

SHING DANG, ,LAM GOL 'KHYAMS PA RNAMS LA LAM STON 'GYUR, ,ZHES
GSUNGS PA LTAR RO, ,DE LTA BAS NA BDAG NYID CHEN PO 'DI LTA BU'I
SKU'I SKYES PA'I RABS KYI GRANGS DANG GO RIM 'DI DANG 'DI LTA BU
ZHES TSUR MTHONG GI SKYE BO SUS KYANG, BTSON BCAD

007 **, ,NAS SMRA BAR MI NUS SO, ,'O NA JI LTAR BSNYAD PAR BYA
ZHIN, RNAM 'GRAL LAS, GNAS GSUM PAR NI 'PHOS PA NA, ,LUNG 'DREN
PA NI MKHAS PA'I LUGS, ,ZHES GZHAL BYA'I GNAS SHIN TU KLOG GYUR RNAMS

LUNG TSAD MA LA BRTEN DGOS PAR GSUNG PAS NA, GNAS 'DI NYID KYANG
DUS GSUM GYI SHES BYA THAMS CAD LA KLOG TU MA GYUR PA'I SPYAN
MNGA' BA PAn CHEN THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA BLO BZANG DPAL LDAN YE
SHES DBANG POS MDZAD PA'I RJE BLA

MA MCHOG GI 'KHRUNGS RABS GSOL 'DEBS SU JI LTAR STZAL BA'I GSUNG
TSAD MA NYID LA BRTEN NAS BRJOD PAR BYA LA, DE YANG 'KHRUNGS
RABS RNAMS KYI RTOGS BRJOD RGYAS PAR MKHAS PA'I GTZUG RGYAN BDAG
GI DPAL LDAN BLA MA DAM PA

'JAM DBYANGS CHOS KYI RGYAL PO DKON MCHOG 'JIGS MED DBANG POS
MDZAD PA'I NGO MTSAR DAD PA'I LJON SHING LAS SHES PAR BYA ZHING,
'DIR NI DON BSDU TZAM TSIGS SU BCAD PA'I DBYANGS KYIS BSNYAD PA
NI 'DI LTAR RO, ,DON DAM

CHOS KYI RO LA RTAG ROL PA'I, ,MI SHIGS DAG PA RDO RJE SNYING
PO'I DPHID , ,KUN RDZOB CIR YANG 'CHAR BA'I MIG 'PHRUL NI, ,'DI
NA SGYU MA'I ROL PA BZHIN DU SNANG, ,'ON KYANG CHAGS LDAN DGU
TSIGS GZHON NU YIS, ,NYI ZLA'I NU MA RGYAS PA

SNGO BSANGS MA'I, ,MGUL PAR 'KHYUD PA'I NGAL BA BSTEN PA BZHIN,
,BDAG 'DRAS TSUL DE SMRA BA BZHAD GAD GNAS, ,DE LTA NA YANG BUS     
PA CHUNG NGU YIS, ,GZHAN GYI RJES SU BZLOS PA'I NGANG TSUL BZHIN,
,TSAD MA'I LUNG LA BRTEN NAS SMRA BA'I 

SGO, ,PHYE BAS CUNG ZAD GLENG BA'I SKABS 'DI RNYED, ,YE SHES
SPYAN GYIS BDEN GNYIS CHOS KUN GZIGS, ,'PHRIN LAS BZANG POS
BSTAN PA'I SNYING PO SPEL, ,LEGS BSHAD SGRON MES THAR LAM GSAL
MDZAD PA, ,THAMS CAD MKHYEN DNGOS L'A LI TA

BDZRA, ,KHYOD NI STUG PO BKOD PA'I ZHING KHAMS SU, ,SAR GNAS
DPA' BO RGYA MTSO'I 'KHOR GYI DBUS, ,RANG DON MTHAR THUG CHOS
KYI SKU BRNYES KYANG, ,THUGS RJE'I DBANG GIS ZHI LA MI GZHOL
BAR, ,DAG DANG MA DAG ZHING KHAMS RAB 'BYAMS SU, 

GDUL BYA'I MOS PA'I RDZING BU THA DAD PAR, ,GANG LA GANG 'TSAM
CHU ZLA'I ROL PA BZHIN, ,'GOG MED SRID MTHA'I BAR DU STON PAR MDZAD,
,{1} THUB DBANG CHOS SPRIN BZANG POS 'JIG RTEN 'DER, ,THEG GSUM
DBYAR RDA DAL GYIS BZHAD PA YIS, ,

RNAM GROL MNGAL KHUR BSKRUN PA'I GTZUG PHUD CAN, ,NYON MONGS
DGRA SDE BCOM PA TZUN ZHES, ,MKHA' LA RGYU SKAR KHROD NA PA
SANGS DANG, ,SA LA RKANG 'THUNG KHROD NA TZAN NA BZHIN, ,THUB
PA'I SLO BA MA'I DBUS NA KHAMS GSUM GYI, ,KUN SPYOR 'DUL BA'I

DPA' PO MCHOG TU GYUR, ,{2} SH'AKYA BSHES GNYEN ZHES GRAGS DED
DPON GYIS, ,'DUS PA'I MAN NGAG GSER GYI GRU SPYAR NAS, ,GRUB
PA'I GO 'PHANG RIN CHEN GLING SON CES, ,GRAGS PA'I BA DAN 'PHAGS
PA'I YUL LAN BSGRENGS, ,KLO SGRUB  CHOS KYI

MDUN SA MDZES PA'I RGYAN, ,RGYAL SRAS PAD DKAR 'DI YI RNAM PAR THAR,
,TSIG GI CHA SHAS PHRA YANG ZLA TSES BZHIN, ,MKHAS MANG BDE
'BYUNG GTZUG GI RGYAN DU GYUR, ,{3} RAB 'BYAMS RGYUD SNGE'I RGYA
MTSOR DBANG BSGYUR BA, ,GRUB MCHOG GDENGS CAN

008 **, ,DPANG PO DAR PAN ZHES, ,GRAGS PA RAB SNYAN GSER GYI
RNGA BO CHE, ,KHOR YUG RI BO'I BAR DU LHANG LHANG BRDUNG, ,RDO
RJE'I RNAL 'BYOR ZAB MO NYI MA'I 'OD, ,'THUNGS PAS LANG TSO
RGYAS PA'I PAD DKAR DE, ,'CHI

MED GRUB PA'I GE SAR SO 'PHRED NI, ,MTHAR BYED GRANG REG DGRA LA
'PHYA BZHIN RGOD, ,{4} THUB BSTAN DROD KYIS BTANG BA'I BHO tA'I
YUL, ,MA RUNGS KLA KLO'I KHA BA RGYUN CHAGS PAR, ,MDO DANG RGYUD
SDE NYID MA'I DKYIL 'KHOR BRGYAB, ,KA BA

DPAL BRTZEGS KHYUNG SDON SKYES KYIS DRANGS, ,DAM CHOS RIN CHEN
SGRON MA TSAR DNGAR NAS, ,BOD YUL RGUD PA'I MUN PA NYIR BCOM

BO JI BZHIN KHUR DU LCI, ,{5} MDO SPYU

SEMS SDE'I MAN NGAG LA BRTEN NAS, ,KUN BZANG GNYUG MA'I RANG
ZHAL MNGON SUM GZIGS, ,SNANG SRID RTEN 'BRAL KUN LA MNGA' BRNYES PA,
,SGRO PHUG PA ZHES GRAGS PA'I 'BRUG SGRA LDIR, ,ZUR RIGS GDUNG
GI RNYOG BRAL RDZING BU'I NANG,,

BZHAD, ,{6} THUGS RJE'I BDAG NYID 'JIG RTEN DBANG PHYUG GI,
,ZHAL BZANG ZLA BA'I 'DZUM 'OD

DRI, ,GRAGS PA'I RLUNG GIS PHYOGS KUN KHYER BA NA, ,'DI NI

ZHES, ,KUN GYIS BSTOD BSNGAS ME TOG PHRENG BAS MCHOD,, {7} BYANG
CHUB SEMS KYI RTZA BA RAB TU BRTAN, ,RLABS CHEN RGYAL SRAS SPYOD

MTSAN GSOL GLANG THANG PA, ,KHE RGYAL BDE THAMS CAD GZHAN LA

'KHON GYI GDUNG RIGS SHAR RI'I RTZER, ,RGYAL SRAS DPA' BO SMRA

BRTZE NUS PAS RGYA BOD HOR GSUM

KUN, ,DBANG DU BSNGUS TE BU RAM SHING PA'I BSTAN, ,'KHOR LO GSUM

LUGS PNGMO KHA' PHYI STE, ,LEGS BSHAD SPRANG RTZI'I DGA' STON STZOL

PA MU TIG DO SHAL GYIS, ,PHYOGS KYI BU MO'I MGRIN PA SKAL BZANG

009 **, ,CHEN CHOS RJE ZHES SU GRAS, ,GANG GI GSANG GSUM BKOD

BSGRING BAR MDZAD, ,RLABS CHEN 'PHRIN LAS NYAL 'GRO GANGS CAN

SNYOD CHOG TER 'JING NA RNAM PAR ROL, ,BSLAB GSUM NOR BU'I BANG

CHEN BZHI, ,GCIG CAR RNAM DPYOD ZHAL DU DRANGS 'DI RMAD, ,GANGS

BSTEN, ,MDO RGYUD MAN NGAG KUN GYI PHA ROL SON, ,NYAMS DANG

NYID, ,{13} PHUN TSOGS NAGS TSAL 'KHRIGS PA'I MDO

SMAD LJONGS, ,GRAGS PA 'OD ZER BRANG 'GRO'I SNYIN PO 'KHRUNGS,
,RNAM DAG KHRIMS KYI DRI BSUNG  ZHIM PO YIS, ,BLO LDAN YID KYI

MI BSRUN SKYE BO'I SMOD TSIG DUG MDA' YANG, ,BSNGAGS BRJOD ME

GANG GI RNAM THAR PNGM'I SPUBS BZHIN GTZANG, ,{14} THUB BSTAN

LEGS 'DOMS PA'I, ,KHYOD KYI LEGS BSHAD PNGM'I PHRING BA NI, ,DUS

010 **, ,BKOD PA 'BYAMS KLAS KYIS, ,'GRO 'DUL 'PHRIN LAS DUS LAS
MI YOL BA, ,'DRIN MCHOG BLA MA'I ZHABS LA PHYAG 'TSAL LO, ,ZHES

DNGOS SU MI 'BYUNG YANG TSAD MA'I LUNG LAS THOS PA'I SKYES RABS

BLA MA 'DI NYID SKYES BU DAM PA MANG PO ZHIG GIS BLA CHEN DGONGS
PA GSAL GYI SKU'I SKYE

PAR GSUNGS TE,  BLA CHEN DAN TIG TU BZHUGS SKANGS THE'U RANG

'ONGS PA'I DUS SUM MDO SMAD KYI LJONGS 'DIR CHOS SDE CHE CHUNG

THOG GYU  THOG 'DEL, ,DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN MANG POS MDO SNGAGS

KYANG DAD PA MA

THOB PAR DE LHA BU'I DUS SU RGYAL PHRAN ZHIG TU SKYES NAS GTZUG
LAG KHANG RNAMS BSREG CING BSHIGS, DGE 'DUN RNAMS BKRAD, DAM PA
DU MA BKRONG BA SOGS BSTAN LA GNOD PA BYED PA'I LOG PA'I SMON
LAM BTAB, BLA    

CHEN GYIS DE LTA BU'I DUS SU DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN ZHIG TU GYUR
NAS RGYAL PHRAN DES BSTAN PA BSNUBS PA SLAR YANG GONG  'PHEL DU
GTONG BA'I THUGS BSKYED DANG SMON LAM RGYA CHEN PO MDZAD DO,
,DUS PHYIS RGYA'I DMAG DPON NYEN GUNG

GES MSO SMAD KYI DGON SDE RNAMS BSHEGS PA RJE BLA MA NGAG DBANG
CHOS KYI RGYA MTSO'I BKA' DRIN LAS ?GONG MA CHEN POS SLAR YANG
SO BAR MDZAD NA 'ANG,  DA LTA'I BAR THABS MKHAS KYI MDZAD PA RGYA
CHEN POS YON RING DU BSKYANGS TE CHOS SRED

GNYIS CHAR NAS N+YA GRO NGHA'I LJON PA BZHIN DU RGYAS PAR BYED PA
PO NI RJE BTZUN BLA MA DAM PA 'DI NYID YIN PAS NA,  LOG PA'I
SMON LAM 'DEBS MKHAN NI NYEN GUNG DANG,  GZHAN RNAMS DES BKRONG
BA'I BLA MA DAM PA'I SKU'I SKYE BA SNGA MA ZHIG TU DON MI ZA

BAS DE'I RNAM THAR MDO TZAM BSHAD NA,  BLA CHEN 'DI SKU SNGA MA
'BRO STAG SNANG KHRI GSUM RJE BYA BAR 'KHRUNGS NAS CHOS LDAN GYI
RGYAL PO'I BKA' BLON MDZAD,  DAM PA'I CHOS 'DZIN  PA'I SMON LAM
RGYA CHEN PO BTAB NAS LO SO LNGA PA LCAGS PHAG

GI LO SKU TSE 'PHOS PA,  CHU PHO BYI BA'I LO TZONG KHA BDE KHAMS
SU PON PO BZA' MI GNYIS KYI BUR SKYE BA BZHES, PHA MAS MU ZUGS
LA 'BAR ZHES BON MING BTAGS, SNGON GYI BAG CHAGS KYI DBANG GIS
CHOS LA DAD NAS SKU NAR SON PA NA

LKOG TU NON 'JAM DPAL BYA BA LAS BZLAS LUNG BLANGS,  KHANG RIN
CHEN RDO RJE  ZHES BYA BA 'PHAGS PA SPYAN RAS GZIGS KYI MTHONG
BA ZHIG LA SEMS BSKYED ZHUS,  SKYI RGYAL BA'I GTZUG TOR LA DAB
TSAD DAD, NAN DGA' LDAN BYANG

011 , ,CHUB LA YO GA GSAN DE'I TSEN BOD DU RGYAL PO GLANG DAR
MAS BSTAN PA BSNUBS PAS,  DPAL CHU BO RI'I SGOM GRVA NA BZHUGS
PA DMAR BAN SH'AKYA MU NE,  GYO DGE 'BYUNG, GTZANG RAB 

SAL LA DANG GSUM GYIS KARMA SHA TAM SOGS 'DUL BA'I DPE CHA DGOS
PA RNAMS BSNAMS NAS NYING PAR YI CHING MTSAN MO LAM BCAD DE BROS
NAS MNGA' RIS SU SLEBS KYANG,  DER BZHUGS MNUS PAS BYANG LAM
BRGYUD DE HOR GYI YUL DU

BYON,  DER DGE BSNYEN SH'AKYA SHES RAB LA BRTEN TE RI ZHIG
BZHUGS KYANG SKAD RIGS MA GCIG PAS BSTAN PAR BYA BA BYED MA NUS
PAS, MDO SMAD LHO'I PE RI TSA MTSO NGOS NAS TSUR BYON TE, RMA
LUNG GI LO RDO RJE BRAG  ,AAN CHUNG GNAM RDZONG,

DAN TIG SHEL GYI YANG DGON RNAMS SU BSGOM ZHING BZHUGS,  DE'I
DUS SU DAN TIG GI RI LA PHYUGS MA 'TSO BA RNAMS KYIS BRAG PHUG
ZHIG NA KHONG GSUM BZHUGS PA MTHONG NAS, DGONG KHA GRONG DU MI
RNAMS LA GLING BA, MU BU GSAL 'BAR

GYIS THOS NAS,  SANG NYIN BLTA BAR PHYIN PAS SLOB DPON GSUM
MTHONG,  'KHOR BA'I SDUG BSNGAL BAS LA NAS THAR PA YI, ,BDUD
RTZIS 'GRO BA'I SDUG SNGAL ZHE BYED PA'I, ,BSTAN PA PHYOGS BCUR
RGYAS PAR BYA BA'I PHYIR, ,DANG POR BDAG

NI RAB TU 'BYUNG BAR BYA, ,ZHES DGONGS NAS RAB TU BYUNG BAR GSOL
BA BTAB PAS, 'DUL BA'I PO TI GTAD NAS 'DI LA LTOS DANG NAR BA TU
'BYUNG NGO GSUNGS, BLTAS PA NA DAD PA LHAG PAR SKYES TE MCI MA
BYUNG NAS RAB TU 'BYUNG BAR

ZHUS PAS,  GTZANG GI MKHAN PO BYAS, GYOS SLOB DPON BYAS TER RAB
BYUNG DANG DGE TSUL DU BSGRUBS TE, MKHAN SLOB KYI MING SPYAR NAS
MTSAN LA DGE BA RAB GSAL ZHES BTAGS PA PHYIS SU THUGS RAB CHE
BAS BLA CHEN DGONGS PA RAB GSAL

ZHES GRAGS SO, ,DE NAS BSNYEN RDZOGS ZHUS PAS DGE SLONG LNGA
MTSANG BAS MI 'ONG GSUNGS PA LA LHA LUNG DPAL GYI RDO RJES GLANG
DAR MA BSAD BOD DU BZHUGS MNUS PAR BROS NAS GLONG THANG DU PHEBS
YOD PA'I DRUNG DU PHYIN TE ZHUS PAS,

NGAS RGYAL PO SDIG CAN BSAD PAS KHA SKONG MI 'ONG,  'ON KYANG
NGAS BTZAL GYIS GSUNG TSE,  RGYA'I DGE SLONG KO  PAD DANG GYI
BAN BYA BA GNYIS BTZAL TI BTAN,  DE NAS SNGAR GYI MKHAN SLOB
KYIS MKHAN PO DANG LAS SLOB BYAS, DMAR GYIS

GSANG STON,  RGYA'I DGE SLONG GNYIS KYIS KHA SKONG BYAS TE BLA
CHEN BSNYEN PAR RDZOGS SO, ,DE NAS BLA CHEN BYANG PHYOGS SU CANG
AIN RTZE MKHAR MI NGAG GHA'I YUL DU BYON TE GO RONG SENG GE
GRAGS LA 'DUL BA GSAN PAS,  LUNG SDE BZHI BSTAN

BCOS DANG BCAS PA GNANG NAS,  BU KHYOD KYIS DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA'I
BSTAN PA TSUL BZHIN DU GSAL BAR GYIS SHIG  ,KHO BO NI RGAS PAS
YUN RING MI 'TSO GSUNG SKAD,  DBUS GTZANG DU SNGAR RGYAL PO
GLANG DAR MAS BSTAN PA BSNUBS NAS

RAB TU BYUNG BA MED PAR BYAS PA'I DBANG GIS SDOM PA BLANG YUL MA
RNYED PA LA,  MDO SMAD DU MKHAS PA MI GSUM DANG BLA CHEN RNAMS
BZHUGS PA THOS NAS,  SDOM PA LEN PAR KLU MES TSUL KHRIMS SHES
RAB SOGS GCAD DBUS KYI MI BCU SLEBS, 

012 **, ,GCANG LA BSNYEN RDZOGS ZHUS PAS NGA RGAS NAS MKHAN PO
MI 'KHYONGS PAS BLA CHEN PO LA ZHUS SHIG GSUNG PA BZHIN ZHUS
PAR,  BLA CHEN GYIS DED BSNYEN PAR RDZOGS NAS LO MA LON PAS
MKHAN PO MI

BTUB GSUNGS BA LA,  GTZANG GIS DMIGS GSAL LA RUNG GSUNGS NAS BLA
CHEN POS MKHAN PO DANG,  GTZANG DANG GYOS LAS SLOB DANG GSANG
STON,  DMAR DANG HVA SHANG GIS BSKOD BYAS TE MI BCU PO BSNYEN
PAR RDZOGS SO, ,DE NAS BLA CHEN

GYI ZHAL NAS,  LO STON MTHU CHE BAS BSTAN PA SRUNGS,  KLU MES
BRTZUN PAS MKHAN PO GYIS,  TSONG DGE BLO RNO BAS STON PA GYIS,
'BRING SKOS MKHAS PAS GNAS GZHI ZUNGS GZHI SOGS KYI BSLAB 
BYA'ANG GSUNG, DE NAS KLU MES KYIS GRUM

YE SHES RGYAL MTSAN LA 'DUL BA NYAN CING BSNGAD,  GZHAN RNAMS
BOD DU THEGS,  PHYI LO KLU MES KYANG BOD DU CHAS TE,  PHEBS KHAR
BLA CHEN LA MCHOD GNAS SHIG ZHUS PAR BON ZHVA 'OB ZHUS SER GYIS
KHA BSGYUR BA GSOL 'PHRO ZHIG GNANG

NAS 'DI GYON LA NGA RJES SU DRAN PAR GYIS GSUNG,  MI BCU PO BOD
DU 'DZOM STE,  SO SOS GNAS GZHI DANG GTZUG LAG KHANG BZUNG RAB
BYUNG DANG BSNYEN RDZOGS KYI SDOM PA TE BSTAN PA DAR BAR BYAS
SO, ,DE LDAN BSTAN PA PHYI DAR ZHES GRAGS

PA'I THOG NI BLA CHEN PO LAS BYUNG PA YIN PAS BKA' DRIN 'DI NI
GANGS CAN PA RNAMS KYIS NAM DU YANG GZHAL BAR NUS PA MA YIN NO,
,BAR SKABS SHIG SHAR  PHYOGS SU LHA RTZE BHIG TIG CES BYA BA,
SNGON GYI LHA RDEN MANG DU BZHUGS PA'I

DGE 'DUN GYI GNAS SHIG TU KVA 'OD MCHOG GRAGS PA DANG MJAL NAS,
SHES RAB KYI PHA ROL TU PHYIN PA'I 'BUM tKI LA SOGS PA DANG,
BYANG CHUB SEMS DPA'I SA LA SOGS PA MNGON PA'I THEGS PA CHEN PO
LO BCU GNYIS SU GSAN NAS, MTSAN

RMA'I RMANG LAM NA GLANG PO CHE GCIG LA BCI BAS NAS NOR BU RIN
PO CHE PHYAG TU BSNAMS NAS,  TSONG 'DUS KUN TU 'GYU GZHING BYON
PA LA MI RNAMS KUN NA RE,  BTZUN PA KHYOD KYI NOR BU BZANG STE,
DA LTAR RE SHIG NYO BA YANG MED, RIN YANG MI THEGS

ZER RO, ,DEN NAS MNAL SAD NAS BSAM PAS,  BSTAN PA RIN CHEN SGRO
MA PHYE STE, ,YON TAN MCHOG GI NOR BYIN YANG, ,MI RNAMS DON DU
MI GNYER BAS, ,RE SHIG NAGS SU GNAS PAR BYA, ,SNYAM DU DGONGS
PA'I SKABS SU, RI DAN TIG DANG NYE

BA NA THE'U RANG SPUN DGU ZHES BYA BA MI MA YIN STOBS DANG LDAN
PA DE RNAMS BLA CHEN PO MTHONG BA DANG DAD PA SKYES TE,  BDAG
CAG GI PHYOGS GANG DANG GANG DGON PA CHEN PO DNGOS GRUB BRNYES
PA MANG DU BYUNG, RTZA BA DANG 'BRAS BU LA SOGS PA

RNYER SLA BA DER 'BYON PAR CI GNANG,  BDAG CAG GIS KYANG KHYED
KYI GROGS DANG DGE BSNYEN DU YANG BGYI'O ZHES ZHU BAS, GNANG NAS
DAN TIG TU BYON NO, ,DE NAS GNAS DER DKON MCHOG LA MCHOD PA RGYA
CHEN PO DANG, CHOS SKYONG LA GTOR MA RGYA CHEN

PO LA SOGS PA MANG DU MDZAD NAS,  BSTAN PA BSRUNG BA SKYOB PA'I
SPYAN SNGA RU, ,THUGS DAM BZHES PA RGYAL SRAS DPA' RNAMS DANG,
,'JIG RTEN SKYOD BA BRDZU 'PHRUL STOBS LDAN PA, ,SKYOB LA GUS
RNAMS BDAG LA STONG GROGS MDZOD, ,CES GSOL

013 **, ,BA BTAB BO, ,DE NAS BDAG NYID CHEN PO DES CIG CAR 'JUG
PA'I RNAL 'BYOR PA ZHES BYA BA DGE BA'O PHYOGS CE YANG MI LOG
RTOG CAN MANG BAS,  DE DAG DAG DAG PA'I CHED DU LHA KHANG DANG
MCHOD RTAN

DPAG TU MED PA BZHENGS, TSON RTZI YANG YUL DER BYUNG,  BZO YANG
RANG NYID KYIS MDZAD NAS 'DUS BYAS KYI DGE BA'I RTZA BA LA
BRTZON PAR MDZAD DO, ,DE LTAR DAM PA'I SPYOD PA DE LTA BUS DANG
PA SKYIS NAS,  SPA GONG YE SHES GYUNG DRUNG ZHES

BYA BA DE 'KHOR MANG PO DANG BCAS NAS DAN TIG TU BYON PA DANG,
BLA CHEN POS DAM PA'I CHOS 'DUL BA NAS GSUNGS PA'I BSLAB PA'I
GZHI RNAMS MRJOD PAS,  RANG NYID KYI SPYOD LAM DE LTA BUS GNOD
ZHING 'GYOD NAS TSUL BZHIN DU RAB TU

BYUNG ,  DE'I RJES SU PAR GNAS BRTAN GRAGS PA ZHES BYA BA RAB TU
BYUNG STE,  SPA PAR GNYIS SO, ,DE BZHIN DU JA PA GRAGS PA DANG
COG CHEN SHES RAB 'BYUNG GNAS GNYIS TE,  JA COG GNYIS SO, ,DE
BZHIN DU BZHAD DPAL GYI RDO RJE ZHES BYA BA

DANG SRAGS RGYA MTSO ZHES BYA BA GNYIS TE,  BZHAD SRAGS GNYIS
SO, ,'AL BA RDOP RJE DBANG PHYUG DANG BSNUBS LA BA SHI DPAL GYI
DBANG PHYUG GNYIS TE,  'AL BSNUBS GNYIS SO, ,ZONG MCHO SKYONG
DANG 'TSUR SHES RAB MCHOG GNYIS TE

ZONG 'TSUR GNYIS SO, ,DE LTAR BLA CHEN SLOB MA'I TSOGS DANG BCAS
PA BSAM GTAN DANG RJES SU MTHUN PA'I DPEN PA'I GNAS YID DU 'ONG
BA DER SPYANGS PA'I YON TAN LA GNAS SHING CHOS KYI DGA' BDE LA
GZHOL BAN,  MTSAN MO'I DUS SHIG

LHA'I DBANG PO BRGYA BYIN LA SOGS PA 'DOD KHAMS KYI LHA DU MA
BLA CHEN NYAN PAR 'ONGS PAS,  LHA'I 'OD KYIS YUL DE DAG DSAL BAR
BYAS PA 'KHOR RNAMS KYIS KYANG MTHONG NGO, ,LHA RNAMS KYIS MCHOD
PA BYAS SHING BLA CHEN GYI DE DAG CHOS KYI BDUD

RTZES TSIM PAR MDZAD PA NA RNAMS KYIS,  BTZUN PA KHYOD NI BZANG
NA MI MA YIN GYI 'KHOR 'DI DAG NI NGAN NO, ,ZHES ZER NAS SONG,
PHYI NYIN 'KHOR RNAMS KYIS MDANGS YA MTSAN PA'I SNANG BA 'DI LTA
BU MTHONG BAS BLA CHEN PO NYID NGES PAR SPRUL PA

ZHIG LAGS SAM ZHUS PAS,  SPRUL PA MA YIN GYI,  BDAG NI THEG PA
CHEN PO LA ZHUGS PA'I SPYOR BA'I LAM PA SNANG BA THOB PA LA
ZHUGS PA'I BNED DGE BA DSAL LA YIN ZHES GSUNGS,  YANG SKABS
GZHAN DU,  DANG PO BUD MED SGOG 'TSONG MA,  ,

BAR DU STAG SNA KHRI SUM RJE, ,DA LTA MU ZU DGE BA GSAL, ,ZHES
BYA BA'I SKYES RAB KYANG GSUNGS SO, ,MKHAS PA MI GSUM NI RE ZHIG
BAR DAN TIG TU BZHUGS NAS SKU TSE'I SMAD DU DMAR DANG GTZANG CHU
CHEN PO'I 'GRAM GYI RI BRAG

DMAR PO ZHIG LA KHANG BU BRKOS TE BZHUGS PAS RI DE LA DMAR
GTZANG BRAG ZHES GRAGS SHING DENG SANG DER CHAGS PA'I GRONG PA'I
MING LA YANG DMAR GTZANG ZHES 'BOD DO, ,GYO DGE 'BYUNG DE DANG
THAG MI RING BA ZHIG TU BZHUGS PAS

LUNG PA DE LA GYO DGE LUNG PA ZHES GRAGS PA DENG SANG ZUR CHAGS
PAS BYID GE LUNG PA ZER RO, ,MTHAR GSUM KA DA LHA'I ZI LING
MKHAR YOD PA'I GNAS 'DIR PHEBS NAS SKU MYA NGAN LAS 'DAS PA'I
GDUNG LA CHOD RTEN BZHENGS

014 **, ,PA PHYIS SU RGYA MKHAR GYI NANG DU TSUD PAS BSNYEN BKUR
SOGS MA BYUNG BAS SA 'BUM TZAM DU GYUR PA DUS PHYIS KYI BAR DU
YOD ZER RO, ,BLA CHEN KYANG SKU TSE'I SMAD DU DMAR GTZAR DU
BYON,  DER GTZUG LAG KHANG DANG RTEN MANG DU BZHENGS,  BRAG LA BRKOS PA'I 
KHANG BU ZHIG TU BZHUGS NAS DGUNG LO BRGYAD CU RTZA BZHI PA SHING 
MO PHAG GI LO MYA NGAN LAS 'DAS SO, ,DE'I TSE ZHAL NAS,  
'PHAGS PA THOGS MED DANG BTZUN

PA MCHE BA'I SDE GNYIS KYIS RGYAL BA'I YUM GYI DGONGS PA MI 'DRA
BAR BKRAL BA DE,  KHO BOS RGYAL TSAB BYAMS PA 'JIG RTEN GYI
KHAMS 'DIR MA BYON GYI BAR DU 'DZAM BU'I GLING 'DI THAMS CAD DU
SKYE BA BRGYAD TZAM LEN DGOS

ZHES KYANG GSUNGS,  BLA CHEN GYIS BSTAN PA'I ME RO GSOS TSUL
PHYIS SU AA TI SHA LA ZHUS PAS,  SO SO SKYE BO LA DE LTA BU'I
'PHRIN LAS MI 'ONG BAS,  BLA CHEN THOB PA CIG YIN NGES GSUNGS
SHING,  'DI NYID KYIS MDZAD PA'I MDO

MCHOD BYA BA GZIGS NAS BOD KYIS 'DI LTA BUG LA SHES,  PndI TAS
MDZAD PA ZHIG YIN 'DUG CES GSUNG SKAD,  SKU GDUNG RIL PO MA
NYAMS PA'I PHYI NAS 'JIM PA'I SKU BRNYAN BZHENGS PA BRAG PHUG
DER BZHUGS PA LA,  DUS PHYIS

BRAG PHUG RDIB KYANG SKYON CUNG ZAD KYANG MA BYUNG,  DE NAS DAD
LDAN RNAMS KYIS GTZUG LAG KHANG BZHENGS NAS DA LTA DER BZHUGS
SO, ,SKU BRNYAN DE NYID KYIS SKYIS BU DAM PA 'GA' ZHIG LA GSUNG
BYON PA DANG,  LAS DAG PA 'GA' ZHIG LA MTHONG SNANG

YA MTSAN CAN BYUNG PA DANG,  SKABS 'GA' ZHIG TU ZHAL MDANGS NAG
POR GYUR PA DANG,  SKU LAS RNGUL THON PA LTA BU BYUNG SKABS DMAG
'KHRUGS SOGS MI LEGS PA DANG,  ZHAL MDANGS BZANG BA'I DUS SU YUL
PHYOGS SU BKRA SHES

PA 'BYUNG BA DANG,  YANG SDUG BSNGAL GYIS NYAM THAG PA 'GA'
ZHIG GIS PHYAG MCHOD SOGS BYAS PAS NYER 'TSE LAS THAR BA SOGS
KYI LO RGYUS CHES MANG ZHING,  RGYUN DU'NG ZHAL RAS KYI MDANGS
MI 'DRA BAR 'GYUR BA DANG,  THUGS KA'I

THAD DU REG NA SKU BYIN DANG MI 'DRA BA'I DROD YOD PA LTA BU
DANG,  NA BZA' PHUL BA LA SKYI CHAGS SHING SKABS 'GA' ZHIG TU
SKU LA 'BYUNG 'GRO BA DANG,  DUS BZANG RNAMS SU TSUL KHRIMS KYI
DRI NGAD KYIS GTZUG LAG KHANG GI PHYI NANG THAMS CAD

KHYAB PA SOGS KYI YA MTSAN DA LTA'I BAR DU DNGOS SU SNANG NGO,
,KYE MA RGYAL NGAN GLANG PO YI, ,LOG SMON SDIG PA'I STOBS DAR
BAS, ,LJONGS 'DI'I THUB BSTAN PAD MA DKAR, ,BRLANG SPYOD MCHE BAS
RTZAD NAS PHYUNG, ,DE TSE BSTAN PA 'BA' ZHIG NI,,

BDE LEGS RTZA BAR GCES DGONGS PA, ,BLA CHEN 'DI YI BKA' DRIN
GYIS, ,SLAR YANG RAB TU GSAL BAR MDZAD, ,TSUL DE 'JIG RTAN KUN
LA SPRON PA'I SLAD, ,DBANG POS PHYOGS KUN SNGAN BA'I 'OD BA KYE
ZHING, ,KHENGS PA BTANG STE GANG

015 **, ,GE DRUNG LHAGS NAS,  GTZUG NOR ZHABS LA GTUGS PA'I LHA
PHYAG BA GYIS, ,RGYAL BSTAN YUNGS 'BRU'I TSAD DU GYUR PA NI, ,MI
RING DPAG BSAM SHING LTAR RGYAS MDZAD PA'I, ,RNAM THAR MCHOG
          
'DIS MKHAS RNAMS YID 'PHROG STE, ,GANG GI RING BSRIL LA YANG SRI
ZHUR BRTZON,,   ,,- GZHAN YANG BDAG CAG GI DPAL LNGAN BLA MA DAM
PA 'DI NYID,  SGRA BSGYUR MAR PA CHOS KYI BLO GROS KYI SKU'I
SKYE BA

YANG YIN TE,  RGYU MTSAN CI LHA BU ZHE NA,  BLA MA DAM PA BOD DU
LAN RJES MA PHEBS SKABS,  NYIN CIG LHA BRIS PA ZHIG LA DPAL
'KHOR LO SDOM PA'I ZHING BKOD 'DRI RGYU'I ZHAL TA GNANG ZHING,
DE DUS KHO BO YANG SKU DRUD DU

YOD PAS,  ZHING BKOD KYI LHA GRAGS SU MAR PA LO TZTSA CIS KYANG
'BRI BAR GYIS,  DE LA RGYU MTSAN ZHIG YOD CES GNANG BA DNGOS SU
THOS,  YANG NYIN GCIG KHO BO MJAL MJAL DU PHYIN NAS SKU DRUNG DU
PHYAG 'BUL SKABS,  RTZED MO'I RNAM

PAS KHYOD KYIS NGA LA PHYAG BYED PA DANG PAS YIN NAM,  MDZES LAM
GYIS YIN ZHES PHEBS PA LA,  DAD PAS YIN MOD ZHUS PAR,  KHYOD DAD
PA'I MIG GIS BLTA SHES SAM, ,DAD PA'I MIG GIS BLTA SHES NA,
,SPYI GTZUG NYI ZLA'I

GDAN STENG DU, ,SGRA BSGYUR MAR PA LO TZTSA DE, ,DAG PA LONGS
SKU'I TSUL DU BZHUGS, ,ZER BA GO YE ZHES GSUNGS,  BDAG LA DE
TZAM LAS MA GSUNGS KYANG BLA MA 'JAM DBYANGS BZHAD PA SPRUL PA'I
SKU RIN PO CHE DANG,  LHA BTZUN NO

MIN HAN LHUN GRUB DAR RGYAS DANG,  DZA SAG BLA MA DGE LEGS NAM
MKHA' SOGS LA,  NGED RANG MAR PA LO TZTSA YIN SRID DE GZHAN LA
YE MA LAB CES DNGOS SU GSUNG SNANG NGO, ,DES NA MAR STON GYI RNAM
THAR MDO TZAM 'GOD NA 'KHRUNGS YUL

NI, LHO BRAG CHU KHYER GYI GRO BO LUNG DPE GSAR DU, YAB MAR PA
DBANG PHYUG 'OD ZER DANG,  YU, RGYA MO BZA' MDO SDE GNYIS KYI
SRAS SU 'KHRUNGS,  YUL GYI SLOB DPON ZHIG LAS YI GE 'BRI KLOG
BSLABS PAS TSEGS MED PAR THUGS SU CHUD,

MTSAN CHOS KYI BLO GROS ZHES BTAGS,  'BROG MI LOTZTSA BA'I DRUNG
DU PHRAL SKAD KYI LOTZTSA BSLABS,  RGYA GAR DU 'BYON PAR BZHED
NAS YO BYAD THAMS CAD GSER DU BRGYUR BAS SRANG BCO BRGYAD TZAM
BYUNG BA BSNAM NAS BAL POR BYON,  LO

GSUM GYI BAR TSA BA GOMS SU BCUG  ,DE'I RING LA SPYI THER BA'I
DRUNG NAS GDAN BZHI LA SOGS PA'I CHOS 'GA' ZHIG GSAN,  DE NAS
RGYA GAR DU BYON PHUL HA RI'I DGON PAR RJE N'A RO PA DANG MJAL
DPAL DGYES PA RDO RJE'I DBANG BSKUR

NAS RGYUR BRTAG GNYIS DANG,  RDO RJE GUR DANG SMBHUt RNAMS GSAN,
GSANG 'DUS ZHUS PAR DED KYIS KYANG SHES MOD,  NUB TU LA KshE
tA'I DGON PA NA PHA RGYUD KYI BDAG PO PnId TA YE SHES  SNYING PO
BZHUGS PAS DER SONG LA ZHUS GSUNGS

PA BZHIN PHYIN NAS DPAL GSANG BA 'DUS PA'I DBANG DANG GDAMS PA
YONGS SU RDZOGS PA DANG,  GZHAN  YANG KRI YA DANG YO GA PHYAG
LEN LAS TSOGS DANG BCAS PA GSAN,  TSUR BYON NAS N'A RO PA LA
MH'A M'A Y'A ZHUS PAS,  DE YANG NGAS

016 **, ,SHES N'ANG DUG  MTSO'I GLING DU KU KU RI PA BZHUGS PA
DE MA RGYUD KYI BDAG PO YIN PAS KHONG LA ZHUS GSUNG,  DE NAS LAM
BAR DU DUG SPRUL DANG GCAN GZAN DANG MI MA YIN GYI 'JIGS PA DANG
BCAS

PAR DKA' SPYAD CHEN POS LHO DUG BTSO'I GLING DU ZLA BA PHYED
KYIS THON,  DPAL ZHI BA BZANG PO DANG MJAL TE SGYU MA CHEN PO'I
DBANG DANG GDAMS NGAG RNAMS RDZOGS PAR ZHUS,  PHYIR PHEBS NAS
N'A RO PAS KYANG TSAR GCIG GNANG,  DE NAS MEE

RTI PA DANG MJAL BAR DGONGS TE DKA' SPYAD SROG DANG BSNGOS NAS
RI ME LTAR 'BAR BA'I DGON PAR BYON, ,MEE TRI PA'I ZHABS LA GTUGS
TE PHYAG RGYA CHEN PO'I GDAMS NGAG BCAS PA DANG DO HA'I BSHAD PA
RNAMS RDZOGS PAR

GSAN PAS SGRO 'DOGS RNAMS CIG CAR DU CHOD PAS,  RJE MNGA' BDAG
CHEN PO'I BKA' DRIN GYIS, ,GZHI CHOS NYID SKYE BA MED PAR RTOGS,
,SEMS STONG PA NYID SPAR ZIN BYAS, ,MI KHO BO'I SPROS PA DE NAS
CHOD, ,CES GSUNGS ,

GZHAN YANG DUR KHROD SOS GLING DU MKHA' 'GRO'I BLA MA LAS GDAN
BZHI DANG,  SI DGHA GLING SOGS GNAS DU MAR MKHA' 'GRO DANG KU SU
LU'I BLA MA MANG PO LAS GDAMS PA SNA TSOGS PA GSAN,  SLAR YANG NA
RO PA'I DRUNG NAS DPAL 'KHOR

LO SDOM PA'I DBANG DANG RGYUD KYI BSHAD PA DANG,  N'A RO'I CHOS
DRUG DANG PHYAG RGYA CHEN PO'I GDAMS PA RNAMS GSAN CING BSGOMS
PAS RTOGS PA BZANG PO 'KHRUNGS,  DE LTAR RGYA GAR DU LO BCU
GNYIS BZHUGS NAS BOD DU BYON PA'I LAM BAR

BAL BOD MTSAMS KYI GRONG KHYER ZHIG TU MNAL LAM DU DPAL GYI RIR
BYON NAS BRAM ZE CHEN POS RA HA DANG MJAL,  PHYAG RGYA CHEN PO'I
BRDA DO RNAMS GSAN PA THUGS LA BZUNG,  LHO BRAG TU PHEBS NAS
RDOG STON CHOS RDOR LA DGYES PA RDO RJE,

MTSUR STON DANG MAR PA MGO LEGS LA GSAN 'DUS KYI DBANG,  RIM
LNGA'I DMAR KHRID,  BA RANG LVA BA CAN LA MA H'A M'A YA'I BSHAD
PA RNAMS GNANG ZHING SO SOS GSER LA SOGS PA'I 'BUL BA RGYA CHEN
PO PHUL,  TSOGS 'KHOR GNANG BA'I BRAL

DU SLOB MA RNAMS KYIS ZHUS NGOR MAR PA RANG GI MTHAR MGUR DU
GSUNG BA NI 'DI LTAR RO, ,RJE RTZOD LDAN DUS KYI RDO RJE 'CHANG,
,DKA' BA SPYAD PA'I SKYES BU MCHOG  ,KUN GYI SPYI BOR THOD BZHIN
'KHOR, ,DPAL N'A RO'I ZHABS LA GUS PAS

'DUD, ,NGA LHO BRAG MAR PA LOTZTSA 'DI, ,LO BCU GNYIS LON NAS
CHOS DANG MJAL, DE SDON SPYANGS KYI BAG CHAGS SAD PAR NGES,
,DANG PO YIG TSANG KA KHA BSLABS, ,THA MA LHO BAL RGYA LA PHYIN,
,LO GSUM BAL

PO'I MTHIL DU BSDAD, ,BYIN RLABS CAN GYI BAL PO LA, ,RGYUD GNYAN
POR GRAGS PA'I GDAN BZHI NYAN, ,CHOS SKYONG DUD SOL LHA MO ZHUS,

,CHU MI ZAN DUG GI CHU LA BRGAL, ,LUS

017 **, ,PA'I DGYIS RDOR DANG, ,BSRI 'PHO MTSAMS SPYOR GYI GDAMS

THOB, ,SHAR DNGOS GRUB KYI CHU BO GANG GA BRGAL, ,RI RAB TU

BZHUGS TSUL GTAN LA PHAB, ,GZHI CHOS NYID DON GYI NGO BO MTHONG,

BRGYUD TSUL YIN, ,GZHAN DUR KHROD MYUL BA'I RNAL 'BYOR DANG,
,SHING DRUNG GNAS PA'I KU SU LU, ,YONGS

SU MA GRAGS 'GA' YOD DE, ,RDZOGS RIM KHA 'THOR MANG DU ZHUS,
,NGO MTSAR CAN GYI SGRUB THABS DANG, ,PHRAN TSEGS KYI GDAMS NGAG
RTZES LAS 'DAS, ,LAM LA KHA RAG GNYOS DANG 'GROGS, ,NGED BAL
PO'I MTHIL DU SLEBS PA'I

TSE, ,NGA LHO BRAG GI MAR PA LOTZTSA DANG, ,KHA RAG GNYOS KYI
LOTZTSA GNYIS, ,LOTZTSA GANG MKHAS GANG MKHAS ZER, ,GDAMS NGAG
GANG CHE GANG CHE ZER, ,YAR BAL BOD MTSAMS SU THON TZAN, ,NOR
ZANG ZING GI SKU BSOD KHONG LA SKYES, ,YUL LA STOD

CHOS GZHIR PHYIN TZAN, ,SGRA BSGYUR GYI GRAGS PA MNYAM PO THOB,
,BOD DBUS GTZANG GI MTHIL DU THON TZA NA, ,GDAMS NGAG GI SNYAN
PA KHO BOS THOB, ,BLA MA GRUB THOB DANG MJAL LAGS PAS, ,GDAMS
NGAG MI CHE'I DOGS MA MCHIS, ,THA SNYAD

LA BYANG CHUB MI RE BAS, ,GZHUNG BSHAD PA KUN JI LTAR DGYES
DGYES MDZOD, ,CES SO, ,DE NAS SNYAN GRAGS DANG SKU BSOD SHIN TU
RGYAS 'KHOR DANG LONGS SPYOD MANG DU 'DUS PAS BDAG MED MA KHA BA
TU BZHAS,  GZHAN YANG PHYAG RGYA MA BRGYAD TZAM YOD

DE DGYES RDOR LHA MO DGU DANG SPYOR BA YIN GSUNGS,  DAR MA MDO
SNGE SOGS SRAS KYANG 'KHRUNGS,  DE NAS GSER MANG PO DANG BCAS
SLAR YANG RGYA GAR DU PHEBS,  DPAL N'A RO PA'I DRUNG DUD GYES PA
RDO RJE'I DBANG RGYAS 'BRIL BSNGUS GSUM,  RGYUD

BRTAG GNYIS,  BSHAD RGYUD RDO RJE GUR DANG SA MBHU t,  RGYAL PO
ANIDRA BO NGHA NES BRGYUD PA'I BDE MCHOG  ,SANGS RGYAS THOD PA'I

NGAG DANG BCAS PA DANG,  GSANG 'DUS KYI DBANG MNYAM

NYID RNAM RGYAL DANG 'GREL PA SGRON GSAL RNAMS GSAN,  MEE TRI PA

LE'I RGYUD RNAMS ZHUS,  GZHAN YANG SNGAR GYI BLA MA THAMS CAD LA
MJAL ZHING CHOS LA DAG THER MDZAD,  N'A RO MEE TRI'I

018 **, ,GTZO BA'I BLA MA RNAMS GSER GYI 'BUL BAS MNYES PAR
BYAS,  RGYA GAR NAS SNGA BOD DU PHEBS SKABS PHYAG DPE RNAMS LAM
BAR DU CHUD ZOS SU SONG 'DI NGES DPE CHA MA MANG DU BSGYUR TE
BRIS SO, ,DE LTAR RGYA

GAR DU LO DRUG BZHUGS NAS BOD DU 'BYON KHAR N'A RO PAS GRONG
'JUG GI GDAMS PA SOGS SNYAN BRGYUD 'GA' ZHIG LEN PAR SLAR YANG
RGYA GAR DU LAN GCIG SHOG GSUNG,  DE NAS BOD DU BYON,  MES STON
TSEN PO LA BDE MCHOG GI DBANG

DANG GDAMS PA GNANG,  RJE BTZUN MI LA SOGS SKAL LDAN GYI BU SLOB
MANG DU  'DUS,  GSER MANG DU BSGRUBS TE RGYA GAR DU 'BYON PAR
CHAS PA LA,  SLOB 'KHOR RNAMS KYIS BSHOL CI BTAB RUNG MA GSAN
PAR RGYA GAR DU PHEBS LAM DU

JO BO RJE BOD DU 'BYON PA DANG MJAL,  RDO RJE 'PHRING BA'I DBANG
GNANG BA ZHAR CHOS SU DSAN,  DE NAS RGYA GAR DU SLEBS PAS,  N'A
RO PA MI BZHUGS PAS,  GSHEGS KHAR MAR PA YONG RGYU YIN KYANG MA
SLEBS PAS 'DI SPROD GSUNG RTEN

SKAL BZHAG 'DUG PA DGE TSUL SHES RAB SENG GIS SPRAD BYUNG BAS,

CHAB MANG DU SHOR,  CI LA THUG KYANG BLA MA DANG MJAL DGOS
DGONGS NAS,  MEE TRE PA'I DRUNG DU PHEBS

NAS ZLA BA GCIG GI BAR TSOGS MCHOD DANG BCAS BLA MA DANG MJAL
BA'I GSOL BA BTAB,  DE BZHIN DU ZHI BA BZANG PO,  RNAL 'BYOR MA
RUS PA'I RGYAN CAN,  GDE TSUL SHES RAB SENGEG, RI RI PA, KA SO
RI PA RNAMS KYI DRUNG DU 'ANG ZLA

BA RE RE LA TSOGS MCHOD DANG BCHAS GSOL PA BTAB PAS DE THAMS CAD
KYIS BLA MA DANG MJAL BA'I LUNG BSTAN STZAL,  DE NAS RI SUL NAGS
KHROD,  GRONG KHYER SOGS PHYOGS THAMS CAD NYUL ZHING DKA' SPYAD
CHEN POS N'A RO PA'I MCHAN NAS

'BOD CING NGU BZHIN BYON PAS SDIG SPYOD KYI RGYAL PO ZHIG GIS
GSER 'PHROG 'DOD PAS BZUNG STE BTZON LA BCUG  ,DE LAS THAR NAS
ZLA BA BRGYAD KYI BAR DU BTZAL BAS MNAL LAM DU MJAL, YANG ZLA BA
GNYIS KYI BAR DU BTZAL BAS MRNYED

PAR SHIN TU NGAL LA ZHING DUB PAS SGYID LUG PA LA NAM MKHA' NAS
BTZON 'GRUS SKYED CIG PA'I SGRU BYUNG BAS ZLA BA GSUM DU BTZAL
BAS N'A RO PA'I ZHABS RJES SHIG RNYED PA LA CHEN POS DE'I RNGUL
SPYI BOR BZHAG CING YANG BTZAL BAS,

NAM MKHA' NAS RJES RNYED PA TZAM LA SNYING PO MED PA'I SGRA
GSAN, DE NAS ZLA BA BZHI BTZAL BAS RI LOG TU RNAL 'BYOR PA GOS
SER PO RA RI GYON PA ZHIG MTHONG BA N'A RO PA YIN NAM MIN SNYAM
PAR, THE TSOM BYAS NA DON MI 'GRUB ZER GAR

SONG MED PAR GSHEGS, DE NAS ZLA BA LNGA'I BAR BTZAL BAS ZHAL
MTHONG YANG ZHIN PA SKYES PAS DE MA THAG YAL SONG, YANG ZLA BA
DRUG BTZAL BAS RNYED NAS,  GSER GYI MndAL PHUL CHOS ZHUS PAS,
MI RO GCIG GI KHOG PA KLAD PA

GSOL GYIN 'DUG PA NAS RTZIBS MAS BLANGS TE GNANG NAS ZO GSUNGS
PA LA SKYUG BLO BAS DE MA THAG YAL,  YANG ZLA BA DRUGM BTZAL BAS
MJAL NAS DED KYANG RJES MA ZIN,  SKABS SHIG THANG CAD PA'I TZUL
GYIS BZHUGS 'DUG PAS GSUNG

019 **, ,GLING 'GA' TZAM GNANG NAS YAL SONG,  'DI YAN NYAMS SNYAD
LA MJAL BA'O, ,DE NAS KYANG DAD  PA SHUGS DRAG POS BTZAL BAS ZLA
BA BRGYAD SONG BAA NA,  RI MUN PA CAN GYI NAGS SU TZNDA NA GYI SDONG

PO'I RTZE MOR DGYES PA RDO RJE LHA DGU'I PAR MJAL,  BLA MA'I SPRUL
PAR SHES NAS GSOL BA DRAG TU BTAB PAS,  DA GZOS N'A RO PA DUR KHYOD 
KYI CHAS KYIS BRGYAN PA ZHIG BYON,  PHA BU'I MDUN NA SLEBS YOD
GSUNGS SKU MNGON

SUM DU BSTAN PAS,  DGA' BA CE DRAGS KHONG NAS YUS PA'I TSIG DANG

SKU LA 'KHYUD DE BRGYAL,  SANGS PA DANG GSER MndAL DU BKOD DE
PHUL, N'A RO PAS

RDZU 'PHRUL GYIS TSOGS RDZAS BKUG NAS TSOGS 'KHOR MDZAD,  MAR
PAS CHOS GNANG BAR GSOL BA BTAB PAS ZHAL GYIS TE DPON SLOB GNYIS
KA PHU LA HA RIR BYON,  LAM BAR DU MKHA' 'GRO MA RNAMS CHOS LA 'KHRON

PA'I CHO 'PHRUL 'JIGS SU RUNG BA BYUNG KYANG GLAGS MA KHEL,  DE
NAS MAR PAS ZHUS PA BZHIN SNGAR MA GSAN PA'I GRONG 'JUG GI GDAMS
PA DANG,  BDE MCHOG MKHA' 'GRO SNYAN BRGYUD KYI CHOS RNAMS GNANG
SNGAR GYI GDAMS

PA RNAMS PHI'I SHUN PA LTA BU 'DI NANG GI YANG SNYING LTA BU YIN
PAS BRGYUD PA BCU GSUM BAR DU CHIG BRGYUD GYIS ZHES BKA' RGYA
MDZAD,  KHYOD RGYA GAR DU YONG THEBS SNGA MA GNYIS LA DUS LA MA
BBAS PAS MA STER,  KHYAD PAR DU CHOS KYI PHYIR

DKA' PA MA SPYAD NA RGYUD LA PHAN MI THOGS,  NGAS KYANG TEE LO
PA'I DRUNG DU DKA' CHEN BCU GNYIS,  DKA' PHRAN BCU GNYIS RNAMS
CHOS 'DI'I PHYIR DU SPYAD PA YIN,  KHYOD KYIS KYANG CHOS KYI
PHYIR LUS SROG LA MA LTOS PA'I DKA' BA SPYAD

'I CHED DU NGA PHRAL DU MA 'PHRAD PA YIN GSUNGS,  DE NAS CHOS
BKA' GNYAN PA DANG BAR CHAD KYI RNAM PAS MAR PA RGYA TSAD KYIS
BSNYUN NAS GRONG LA KHAD PA BYUNG YANG N'A RO PA'I BYIN RLABS
KYIS BSNYUN LAS GROL,  N'A RO PAS CHOS DRUG RDO RJE'I MGUR

GSUNG,  DE NAS MEE TRI PA'I DRUNG DU BYON NAS BDE MCHOG DANG
DGYES PA RDO RJE'I DBANG ZHUS,  'DE RES RGYA GAR DU LO GSUM
BZHUGS TE BOD DU BYON,  BAL YUL RIN CHEN TSUL GYI GTZUG LAG
KHANG DU,  BLA MA SEN TA PA LA CHOS 'GA' ZHIG

GSAN SKABS MNAL LA MA MEE TRI PA SEN GE LA CHIBS NAS MDUN GYI
NAM MKHAR BYON PA LA GSOL BA BTAB PAS PHYAG RGYA CHEN PO BRDA'I
DON BSTAN,  DE NAS BOD DU PHEBS PA'I LAM DU SLOB RNAMS KYIS
BSNYEN BKUR DANG DE DAG LA RGYA

GAR DU BYON TSUL GYI MGUR MANG DU GSUNG,  PHUG RON DANG LUG GU
DANG SHA BA'I RO SOGS LA DNGOS SU PAS GRONG 'JUG MDZAD NAS GDAMS
NGAG LA YID CHES PAR MDZAD,  SRAS DAR MA MDO SDE 'BUM LA GDAMS
NGAG MANG PO DANG KHYAD PAR

GRONG 'JUG GI GDAMS PA GNANG BAS,  DAR MA RTAS BRDABS NAS GRONG
KHAR PHUG RON GYI RO LA GRON 'JUG MDZAD DE RGYA GAR DU BRAM ZE'I
BU'I RO LA ZHUGS PA TI PHU GSANG SNGAGS KYI SDONG ZHES GRAGS SO,
,DE NAS BLA MA MAR PA NYED

020 **, ,KYIS GZHUNG  DANG GDAMS NGAG GI DKOR MDZOD KHA PHYE STE
BU SLOB RNAMS LA NYIN 'CHAD CING MTSAN BSGROM DU BCUG NAS KUN

DBANG NGE,  RNGOG STON CHOS RDONG,  MES STON TSON PO,  MI LA RAS

BKA' BBAS,  KHYAD PAR DU MI LA LA SLOB MA GZHAN SU L'ANG MA GNANG

KYI RABS KYI GDAMS NGAG DANG BYIN RLABS KYI BRGYUD PA KHYED

DKA' BA SPYAD PA'I DBANG DU

BYA SAN,  SNGA PHYIR RGYA GAR DU LAN GSUM BYOM PAS DE DAG GI
SKABS SU MAR PA RANG GI MGUR LAS,  NGA BAL PO'I LAM DU ZHUGS TZA
NA,  ,GCAN 'PHRANG DAR CHUL THAR DUS MED, ,NAGS MTHUG PO CIG LA
DUS MED, ,SHING SDONG

PO MI RO RENGS PA 'DRA, ,LAM DE KUN GYI SDUG BSNGAL MTHONG TZAN,
,BYA DGUNG DU 'PHUR BA GSHOGS PA 'DAR, ,ZHES DANG,  NGA DE NAS
RGYA GAR DU PHYIN TZA NA, ,MTHA' 'KHONG KYI JAG PA SHI SKYID PA,
,SROG CI BDER THON PA'I RE MA MCHES, ,GCAN 
         
GZAN PHYI NGAR SKAD THOS TZAN, ,LUS GTZANG SAR THON PA CUNG MA
BSAMS, ,SPRUL SPAL CHEN GYI KHA RLANGS MTHONG PA'I TSE, ,YID
BRTAN PAR PHYIN YANG GOM TSUGS 'KHYOR, ,LAM DE KUN 'JIGS PA
MTHONG BA RNAMS, ,DUS DA LTA DRAN YANG GLO

SNYING 'DAR, ,CHU GRAGS PA CAN GYI GA GA BRGAL, ,ZHES DANG,
CHOS SNYING NAS 'TSOL BA'I GDUNG SEMS KYIS, ,YUL RGYA GAR SHAR
NUB CHU BZHIN MYUL, ,THANG CHEN PO CIG LA CHOD DUS MED, ,ME 'OBS
KYI THANG LA PHYIN NO SNYAM, ,YID CHOS LA

BAS MA KYANG SNYING RLUNG 'PHYO, ,NAD 'TSO BAR DKA' BA'I TSAD
PAS THEBS, ,DE SHI DE CHAD BCU GSUM BYUNG, ,KHA CHEM TSIG GSUM
BZHAGS MED, ,DBUGS  'GYU BA CHAD PA LAN GAUM MYONG, ,DUS DE KUN
GYI SDUG SNGAL MTHONG TZAN, ,SDANG

BYIN GYIS NI LHA RNAMS MEG MOG POR BYAS SKYE RGU'I GDREN BYED PDMAR
NGO MTSAR ZE

'BRU'I PHRENG BA SPEL, ,GNAG GSUNG DRUG CU'I DBYANGS LDAN DBYAR
SKYES RNGA GSANG PHYOGS KUN BZHAD PAS TSANGS PA'I DBYANGS SNYAN
SKYENGS BYAS SKAL BZANG RNA BA'I DPAG BSAM 'DAB RTZER BDUD
RTZI'I ZIGS MA CIR YANG 'THOR, ,GANG THUGS

027 **, ,'GYUR MED SNYING RJE'I ROS GANG SPROS KUN NYER ZHI'I
CHOS DBYINGS ROL PAS KUN GSAL SGEG MO'I KHENGS 'PHROG BDEN GNYIS
BYA'I DKYIL 'KHOR KHYON KUN CAR GSAL BAR GZIGS,  ,

GSANG BA GSUM LDAN RJE BTZUN BLA MA ROL PA'I RDO RJE'I ZHABS SEN 
'CHAR KA'I GZIM MDANGS DREGS LDAN GTZUG NOR 'OD DANG 'DRES PA DE 
YIS BDAG PDOM RTAG TU SKYONGS, ,GANG YANG 'DI NA 'JIG RTAN PHAN
BDE'I SNANG BA SNYIGS MA LNGA YI

MUN PAS RIM GYIS ZOS, ,LAM DANG LAM MIN JI BZHIN GSAL BYED 'GRO
BA'I NYI MA ZHING GZHAN NUB KYI RI BOR BZHUD, ,MA RIG GNYID KYIS
RAB NON 'GRO RNAMS LAS SNANG RMI LAM GRONG DU SDUG BSNGAL BTZON
RAR BCINGS, ,RMONGS BA'I GNYID

SLONG CHOS KYI NYID KYANG GLEGS BAM KHANG BUR SGRA MED GZIM PAR
GYUR, ,DE TSE RGYAL BA'I CHOS TSUL KUN BZUNG NAS, ,LUS CAN PAN
BDE'I SGO 'PHAR BRGYA 'BYED PA'I, ,RLABS CHEN SMON LAM RING NAS
MDZAD PA YI, ,RGYAL SRAS DPA' BO

MCHOG GIS ZHING 'DI BZUNG, ,MI BZAD SNYIGS MA LNGA YI MTHU
RDZOGS BAS, ,SNYING STOBS CHE LDAN RGYAL SRAS GZHAN RNAMS KYIS,
,BTANG SNYOMS BZHAG PA'I BSTAN 'GRO'I KHUR CHEN PO, ,GANG GI
THUGS RJE'I KHYOGS LA CI BDER BLANGS, ,KHYAD

PAR BLO BZANG RGYAL BSTAN YID BZHIN NOR, ,LUMG DANG PAS BYI DOR
LEGS BSGRUBS TE, ,THOS BSAM SGOM PA'I RGYAL MTSAN RTZER MCHOD
NAS, ,'DZAD MED PHAN BDE'I DGA' STON CHAR DU BSNYIL, ,DGE LEGS
SHEL GYI RVA BAS YONGS

SKOR DBANG PHYOGS 'CHI MED GRONG KHYER DU, ,DREGS LDAN BYE BA'I
BZHIN RAS SNOD GYUR NOR BU'I KHRI 'PHANG MTHON PO RU, ,YE SHES
SPYAN STONG LDAN GANG BZHUGS PAS BSTAN 'DZIN LEGS BRIS MA LUS
PA, ,NAG PHYOGS LHA MIN GYUL LAS RGYAL PA'I

DGA' STON NYAMS PA MED PAR GYUR, ,CHOS KYI RDO RJES MDO SMAD
SMAN LJONGS NA, ,GANG GI NGO MTSAR YON TAN RJES DRAN NAS, ,LAG
PAD SPYI BO'I TSAL DU NYER ZUM STE, ,RTOGS BRJOD MGRIN PA'I
RGYUD MANG 'DI BSGRINGS SO, ,BSHES GNYEN DU MA'I ZHAL GYI

BDUD RTZIS THUGS KYI BUM BZANG YONGS GANG MDO SNGAGS GZHUD LUGS
RGYA MTSO'I PHA ROL SON, ,'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM LAS YI STENG 'DIR
'GRAN ZLA DANG BRAL MKHAS PA'I RTZER SON GRUB PA'I GO 'PHANG
MTHON POR GSHEGS, ,'PHRIN LAS BZANG POS

BSTAN 'GRO'I PHAN BDE BLAR SPEL 'DZAM GLING CHE RGUS ZHABS KYI
PAD MA GUS PAS SPYI BOR MCHOD, ,'DI DAG NGO MTSAR GTAM GYI GLING
GZHI NYID DE BDAG BLO'I RTZAL GYIS CI TZAM SPONGS PA DE BRJOD
PAR BYA, ,DA NA SI BCAD GNYIS PA SKU TSE 'DI

NYID KYI RNAM PAR THAR PA RGYAS PAR 'GOD PA LA 'JUG PAR BYA STE,
 'DI LA GNYIS,  DNGOS DANG,  DON BSDU BA'O, ,DANG PO NI,  DE
YANG RJE BLA MA DAM PA 'DI NYID GANG DU 'KHRUNGS PA'I YUL NI,
MDO SMAD TZONG KHA'I BYANG PHYOGS KYI SA'I CHA, 

SNGON GYI DUS SU HOR RGYAL POS 'JAM DBYANGS SA PAn DANG,  CHOS
KYI RGYAL PO 'PHAGS PA SOGS GDAN DRANGS NAS CHOS KYI 'KHOR LO
BSKOR ZHING GTZUG LAG KHANG DANG DGE 'DUN GYI SDE MANG DU BTZUGS
PA'I GNAS LANG GRU'U SNGE BZHI ZHES GRAGS

028 **,  ,PA LAS,  NUB PDOM'I SNGE'I SA CHAR GTOGS PA'I 'BROG
GNAS,  GTZANG ZHING DBIN LA YID DU 'ONG BA, ,LHA SHUG GI NAGS
TSAL DANG RTZI SMAN ME TOG SNA TSOGS PAS KHYAB CING,  RGYAB RI
BRAG DKAR DUNG

RI SPUN BDUN DU GRAGS PA SBYIBS LEGS LTA NA SDUG PA'I BRAG RI HA
CANG MI CHE BA BDUN TSAR DU BSGRIGS PA,  SPANG LJONGS DANG RI
BRAG 'BAB CHU LA SOGS PA'I DGE MTSAN THAMS CAD TSANG BA'I PHUN
SUM TSOGS PA'I GNAS LUNG PA'I DBYIBS

DANG RTAGS MTSAN SOGS 'OG TU 'BYUNG PA'I LUNG BSTAN RNAMS DANG
SHIN TU MTHUN PA ZHIG GO, ,RIGS RUS NI HOR YIN TE,  RJE RGYAL BA
GNYIS PA'I 'KHRUNGS YUL MDO SMAD TZONG KHA'I PHYOGS SU SNGON DUS
SU CHI KYA DOR RTAN PO ZHES

GRAGS PA'I BRGYUD PA DA LTA CHI KYA DPON POR 'BOD PA DE'I 'BANGS
SU GTOGS PA'I KHYIM GRANGS MI NYUNG MI TZAM YOD PA'I GRONG SDE
'GA' ZHIG YOD PA LAS,  YAB NI SDE DE KA'I SNGAGS PA ZHIG YIN
KYANG,  GNAS 'PHOS TE LANG GRU'U PHYOGS

SONG NAS 'BROG KHYIM BZUNG BA LA PHYOGS DER SNGAGS PA LA TSANGS
PA ZER BAS CHI KYA TSANGS PA GU RU BSTAN 'DZIN BYA BA,  RANG
BZHIN DRANG ZHING DPA' RTZAL DANG RTUL PHOD PA,  MA nI DUNG
PHYUR SONG ZHING,  RDO RJE 'JIGS BYED KYI RNAL 'BYOR CHAG

MED THUGS DAM DU MDZAD PA ZHIG YIN,  YUM NI BU SKYID BYA BA MED
KYI SKYON LAS 'DAS SHING DAD PA DANG LDAN PA DGE SPYOR LA RTAG
TU BRTZON PA ZHIG STE,  YAB YUM DE GNYIS KYI SRAS SU RAB BYUNG
BCU GNYIS PA'I GSER 'PHYAD ZHES PA

ME MO BYA'I ZLA BA DANG PO'I TSES BCU dA KI 'DU BA'I DUS KHYAD
PAR CAN GYI RJE BLA MA 'DE NYID SU BSTAMS PAR GYUR TO, ,'JAM
DPAL RDO RJE'I RNAM 'PHRUL SA SKYA PA, ,GNAS LNGA RIG PA'I PAn
CHEN H'A NNDA'I, ,ZHABS PAD NYER

BKOD DAM CHOS GSER SPYANGS KYI, ,'KHOR LO LAN GRANGS STONG DU
BSKOR BA'I GNAS, ,PHUN TSOGS SNGE BZHI SA YI DGE MTSAN BCU,
,YONGS TSANG LANG GRU'U ZHES GRAGS MndA LA, ,GRONG DANG GRONG
KHYER TSOM BUS MDZES PA NI, ,MTHO RIS

DGA' 'TSAL SA LA 'PHOS 'DRA YOD, ,DER NI SPANG LJONGS GTZANG
MA'I DU K'U LA'I, ,NYER KLUBS PHU CHU'I 'OG PAGS SNYAN SGRA
'BYIN, ,ME TOG DO SHAL 'CHANG BA'I DBYIG 'DZIN MA, ,PHUN TSOGS
LANG TSO'I DPAL YON DOMS PA BZHIN,,

'KHRI SHING SNA CHOGS LDEM LDEM GAR BYED CING, ,BUNG BA GZHON NU
DAR DIR GLU DBYANGS LEN, ,SPU SDUG 'DAB CHAGS MGRIN PA'I RJA
RNGA BRDUNG, ,BAG PHEBS RI DAGS BANG RTZAL 'GRAN CING RTZE, ,DUNG
RI DKAR PO 'PHAGS PA'I NOR GYI

GRANGS, ,BKRA SHES SBYANGS SNYAN SGROGS LA 'GRAN PA BZHIN, ,LHA
SHUG NAGS KYIS PHYOGS MCHAMS GTIBS PA NI, ,BYED POS GTZANG BYAD
RDZAS SU BKRAM PA BZHIN, ,DE LTA'I SA YI THIG LER NI, ,RIGS RUS
CHO 'BRANG MI DMAN ZHING,,

YON TAN NOR BU'I RGYAN 'CHANG BA'I, MI MCHOG THABS SHES 'BREL BA
LAS, ,SGYU 'PHRUL MAR MTSUNGS YUM GYI SPRIN RUM NAS, ,YID 'ONG
SPRUL SKU'I NYI GZHON SHAR BA NA, ,SKAL BZANG 'GRO BA'I 'DRIN
BYED PDMA NI, ,NGO MTSAR ZE'U 'BRU'I

029 **, ,PHRING PA 'RDZIN PAR GYUR, ,CES BYA BA NI BAR SKABS KYI
TSIGS SU BCAD PA'O, ,KHYAB BDAG RDO RJE SEMS DPA'I NGO BO DANG
LA LDAN BLA MA DAM PA YE SHES BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME DPAL BZANG
PO'I RNAM PAR THAR

MDO TZAM BRJOD PA DGE LDAN BSTAN PA'I MDZES RGYAN LAS,  SKU
BLTAMS PA'I LE'U STE DANG PO'O,,   ,   ,,SNGA PHYIR RMI LTAS
DANG RTAGS YA MCHAN PA BYUNG TSUL NI,  SNGAR LO MNGAL LAN BZHUGS
SKABS YUM GYI RMI LAM

DU MO RANG GI LUS GSER DU GYUR PA LAN 'GA' ZHIG TU RMIS PA DANG,
KHO NA GSER GYI RI GCIG YOD SNYAM BYUNG BA RMIS,  YAB KYI ZHANG
PHO RAB 'BYAMS PA CIG SHA RA THAL ZER BA'I SA CHAR SOG PO'I
SPYIN BDAG GCIG GI NANG LA

SDOD SKABS DGUNG GCIG RMI LAM LA,  7SPRUL SKU'I 'KHRUNGS BRAG
DKAR ZER BA'I LUNG PA'I LHO PHYOGS TSA BBAS GCIG GI SA CHAN
GLANG MDO ZER BA'I LUNG PA CIG YOD PA DE KA'I THAD KYI NAM MKHA'
NAS SPRIN SHIN TU STUG PO

'KHRIGS PA'I NANG 'BRUG SKAD SHIN DU CHE BA ZHIG SGROGS BZHIN
PAR,  7SPRUL SKU BLTAMS PA'I GNAS NA BRAG DKAR PO MTHO ZHING
MDZES PA CIG YOD PA DANG NYE PA NA KHA DOG SNA LNGA PA'I 'JA'
TSON BCAS BRAG THIM PA DANG BRAG LA

SGO GCIG BYUNG,  SGO DE NAS RJE BTZUN BYAMS PA PHEBS RGYU RED
ZER BAS,  KHO RANG DANG KHONG GI AA KHU DGE SLONG AA KHU RGAD PO
GCIG DANG BCAS PAS DAD GUS CHEN POS PHYAG MCHOD BYED PA CIG
RMIS,  SANG NYIN DE PHYOGS SUN NAG SHU'U BLA

MA ZER BA SMYUNG GNAS RANG LA THUGS DAM SHIN TU 'GRUS PA GNANG
MKHAN CIG YOD PA DE LA ZHUS PAS,  KHONG GIS RMI LAM SHIN DU
LEGS,  KHYED TSO'I BRAG DKAR ZER BA'I SA CHA DE LA SKYES BU DAM
PA SHIN TU GRAGS CHE BA CIG DNGOS SU 'BYON PA'M,

DE 'DRA CIG GI SPRUL SKU PHEBS PA'I LTAS YIN PA 'DRA GSUNGS,
7SPRUL PA'I SKU 'KHRUNS BA'I LO DE LA GNAS THUGS DAM DU MDZAD
MKHAN GYI BLA MA DES NUB GCIG RMI LAM DU CHA KYI TSANGS PA'I
KHYIM NA SENG GI MO GCIG GIS SENG PHRUG LA NU

MA BSNUN PHYIN 'DUG ZER  BA CIG BYUNG BAR,  KHONG GIS SENG GI'I
NUM LAG MTHIL DU YOD ZER BA THOS PAS BDEN MI BDEN BLTA DGOS
SNYAM NAS SONG BAR SENG GI MO DE BROS NAS STON PA CIG RMIS,
SANG NYIN CHE KYI TSANGS PA ZER BA CIG YOD

MED MI 'GA' ZHIG LA DRIS PAR SHES MKHAN 'GA' ZHIG GIS YOD ZER,
DER KHO SKU DRUNG NGU BOS NAS KHYOD LA BU 'DRA AE YOD CES DRIS
PAR KHO RANG GIS BU LO BCU LON PA GCIG DANG,  BYIS PA ZLA BA
GSUM BZHI 'GRO BA GCIG YOD ZHUS

PAR,  BLA MAS KHYOD RANG GI BU CHUNG DE NGA'I RMI LTAS LA DPAG
NA GANG ZAG RANG DGA' BA CIG MIN 'DUG PAS,  GTZANG SPRA GANG
THON THON DANG,  SKUR RIM LA RIM RIM GYIS GSUNGS NAS SKOL JA
SOGS KYI GNANG SPYIN KYANG MDZAD,  DGUNG LO

GNYIS GSUM BZHES DUS NYIN GCIG KHYIM DU GRA PA KHA SHAS KYIS
CHOS 'DON ZHIG BYED SKABS,  'DON GYIN YOD PA'I DPE CHA RNAMS
SPRUL SKUS PHAR LEN TSUR LEN MANG PO MDZAD PA YAB KYIS LAN 'GA'I
BAR BZLOG KYANG MA GSAN PA LA

030 **, ,YAB KHROS NAS PHU THUNG GIS BRDUNG PAS BSHUM BZHIN DU
KHYIM SGO NAS PHYIR THON,  DAR GCIG NA BSHAM 'PHRO BCAD NAS NAM
MKHA' LA SPYAN CE RE GZIGS TE,  AA MA ZHES BOS NAS NAM MKHA'

NA,  RJE RIN PO CHE,  AU RGYAN RIN PO CHE, BLA MA RIN PO CHE
RNAMS BZHUGS 'DUG  ,AA PHABS NGA BRDUNG BYUNG ZHES MA LAB PA SKU
RIM 'DON MKHAN GYI MI TSOS THOS NAS YAB LA BU CHUNG 'DIR NGA GA
BA ZHIG MIN 'DUG PAS PHYIN CHAD

DE 'DRA MBYED CES LAB 'DUG  ,NYIN GCIG NGAS KHYED RNAMS LA DBANG
SKUR BYED CES,  BUM PA ZHIG YOD PA THAMS CAD KYI MGOR 'JOG CING,
DBANG BSKUR RDO RJE CHEN PO STE, ,KHAMS GSUM KUN GYI PHYAG BYAS
PA, ,SANG

RGYAS KUN GYI GSANG GSUM GYI, ,GNAS LAS BYUNG BA SPYIN PAR BYA,
,ZHES PA'I TSIGS BCAD DAG CING GSAL BA THOGS MED GSUNGS PAS DE
NA YOD PA'I SER SKYA THAMS CAD SHIN TU HA LAS SHING NGO MTSAR
BAR GYUR TO, ,GANG

THUGS DPAL GYI BE'U'I GRA GCIG TU, ,CHOS KUN RJOGS PAR CHUD PA'I
LHA MCHOG LA, ,MKHYEN PA'I GTER ZHES GRAGS PA NYID NI, ,BYIS
PA'I ZOL GYIS MDO SMAD LJONGS SU BYON, ,GANGS CAN GRUB MTHA'I
YANG RTZE DGE LDAN PA'I,,

RING LUGS 'DI YIS GSAL BAR BGYID ZHES, ,YAB RJE 'JAM DPAL SNYING
PO THUGS DGYES TE, ,RINGS PA'I TSUL GYIS 'DZUM ZHAL KHYOD LA
BSTAN, ,GANG GI SKU YI BAR CHAD NGAS BAS ZHES, ,'DZAM BU'I GLING
NA CHE BA'I RIGS SNGAS

'CHANG, ,SNANG SRID ZIL GNON PDMA K'A RA YIS, ,DGYES ZHAL DNGOS
SU BSTAN NAS BYIN GYIS BRLABS, ,BDAG NI RGYAL KUN SNYING RJE'I
MA MA STE, ,DAM CHOS 'O MAS RGYAL SRAS GZHON NU KHYOD, ,BSKYANG
BAR BYA ZHES 'PHAGS MCHOG 'JIG RTEN DBANG,,

DUR SMRIG 'DZIN PA'I GZUGS KYIS KHYOD DRUNG BYON, ,NA TSOD SGO
NGA'I SPUBS RGYA MA GROL KYANG, ,DAM PA'I RANG RTAGS DBYANG
SNYAN SGROGS PA YIS, ,RGYAL SRAS KA LA NGES RNYED NAS, ,SKYE
RGU YA MTSAN BSNGAGS PA BRJOD LA BREL, ,RJE NGAG

DBANG BLO BZANG CHOS LDAN PA'I SKU'I SKYE BAR NGES PA RNYED PA'I
TSUL NI,  DGUNG LO GNYIS BZHES SKABS NYIN GCIHG NGA BLA MA LCANG
SKYA YIN GSUNGS SHING,  LHO PHYOGS LA PHYAG MDZUB KYIS BSTAN NAS
PHA GIR DGON PA CHEN PO YOD,  NGA DER SONG

NAS BLA MA BYED RGYA YIN ZHES SOGS SNGON NASD RJES DRAN GYI
GSUNG MANG DU BYON 'DOG CING,  DE DUS YUM GYIS ZA MA GRIB CAN
CIG ZOS PAR BRTAN,  SKU GRIB KYI RNAM PAS SKU GZUGS THAMS CAD
SHU BAS KHYAB NAS 'O BRGYAL SE BA BYUNG BAR

MGON PO'I RNAL 'BYOR BA YIN PA'I M'A BLA MA ZER BA CIG LA BRTAG
PA ZHUS PAR,  GRIB BYUNG BA YIN 'DUG PAS BYABS KHRUS GANG MANG
DANG SKU RIM 'GA' ZHIG GYIS ZHES PHEBS NAS YAB YUM GNYIS KYIS
ZHAL GZIGS RI KHROD KYI BLA MA

'DAN MA CHOS RJE ZER BA'I SKU ZABS LA BYAS KHRUS ZHU BAR SANG
'GRO BAR THAG BCAD PA'I DGUNG MO DE LA 'DAN MA BLA MA'I RMI LAM
LA NYI MA GZAS ZIN 'DUG PA LA GIS LA RANG DBU MDZAD NAS RI KHROD
PA THAMS CAD TSOGS NAS KHROS GSOL BGYIS

031 **, ,PAS GZA' LAS GROL NAS 'OD GSAL PO BYUNG BA ZHIG RMES,
DE'I SANG NYIN BU CHUNG BYABS KHRUS LA KHYOR YONG BAR BLA MAS
RMI LTAS LA DBAGS NA 'DI GANG ZAG RANG GA BA MIN 'DUG CING,
BYABS KHRUS KYIS

KYANG PHAN RGYU YIN 'DUG DGONGS NAS,  RNAM 'JOMS KYI BYABS KHRUS
BRGYA TSAR,  GZHAN YANG RJES GNANG BKA' BSGO SOGS MANG DU STZAL
BAS BSNYUN LAS GROL 'DUG CING,  DE PHYIN CAD BLA MA DES KHONG
RANG GI GONG MCHOS RJE 'GANG CHEN

ZHIG ZHING LA PHEBS PA DE'I SKU SKYE YIN PAR RE NAS SKU RIM SOGS
KYANG GANG DRAG MDZAD,  M'A BLA MA LA KHONG RANG GI BLA MA'I SKU
SKYE YIN MIN GYI BRTAG PA ZHUS PAR,  BU CHUNG DE LO BZHI THOG NAS 
GSAL KHA NYI MA SHAR 'DRA ZHIG YONG,  DA LTA 

GSAL KHA MI THUB ZER BA BBAS 'DUG  ,DE RJES SKABS SHIG ZHAL GZIGS       
RI KHROD KYI BLA MA'I RMI LAM LA CHU MDOG SNGO ZHING SHIN TU
DANGS PA ZHIG BKRA SHIS THANG ZER BA'I LUNG PA DE KHYAB NAS RIM
GYIS CHE RU 'GRO BAR,  KHONG GI BSAM PA

LA 'DI HA CANG CHE RU SONG NA LUNG PA 'DIR MI SHONG BA 'DUG PAS,
PHYOGS GZHAN ZHIG TU DRANGS DGOS SNYAM LAG TU 'KHAR GSIL CIG
THOGS 'DUG PA'I YU BAS BRAG CIG LA BRGYAB NAS BYAMS PA GLING DU
SONG ZHIG BYAS PAR,  'KHAR GSIL

BRGYAB PA'I SHUL DU BUG PA ZHIG THON PA'I NANG DU CHU THAMS CAD
LHO PHYOGS SU LHAG MED DU BSHAR SONG BA CIG RMIS PAS,  BLA MA
DANG YAB YUM TSOS CHU 'DI 'GRO BA RNAMS 'TSO BA'I RTEN DU GYUR
PA YIN PAS,  BU CHUNG 'DI RANG GA BA CIG

MIN 'DUG KYANG NGA RANG TSO'I BLA MA'I SKU SKYE RANG AE YIN,
BYAMS PA GLING ZER BA CIG NAS RTZAD GCOD MKHAN BYUNG NA NGES PAR
DER 'GRO BA 'DRA ZHES GLING,  SNGA PHYI'I LO RGYUS DE RNAMS RIM
GYIS DGON LUNG DU GRVA RIGS RNAMS KYIS THOS PAS, 

BLA MA DE NYID KYI SKU'I SKYE BA PHAL CHER 'DI RANG YIN 'DRA
SNYAM PA BYUNG 'DUG NA'NG,  DOGS GNAS GZHAN 'GA' ZHIG KYANG YOD
'DUG PAS THAG MA CHOD PA'I BAR SKABS SHIG TU,  DGON LUNG GI SLOB
CHUNG ZUR PA RI KHROD LA BZHUGS NAS THUGS

DAM DGE SPYOR LA SHIN TU BRTZON ZHING, ?SKU ZHABS DE NYID LA MI
PHYED PA'I DAD PA DANG LDAN PA RAB 'BYAMS PA BSTAN 'DZIN ZER BA
ZHIG GIS DGUNG GCIG RMI LAM DU DGON LUNG GI RGYAB RI'I THAD NAS
NYI MA'I DKYIL 'KHOR 'OD ZER NYI MA GZHAN

LAS KHYAD PAR SU 'PHAGS PA CIG SHAR 'DUG PAR BLTAS PAS,  DKYIL
'KHOR GYI KHYON TSON GSUM BZHI TZAM GYI TSOD YIN PA LA 'OD ZER
GZAN DANG 'DRA BA ZHIG 'DUG PA RMIS NAS,  SANG NYIN KHONG RANG
GI ZLA BO CHO LA,  SPRUL SKU 'KHRUL

MED LANG GRU'U PHYOGS KYI DE KA YIN 'DUG KYANG,  'THEN KHYER
'DIS CI 'DRA RANG YONG ZHES GLIN 'DUG  ,DE YANG RJE BLA MA 'DI
NYID KYI SNGA MA YONGS RDZOGS BSTAN PA'I MNGA' BDAG NGAG DBANG
BLO BZANG CHOS LDAN DPAL BZANG PO DE NYID SKU DNGOS KYI

GDUL BYA RDZOGS NAS RE ZHIG ZHI BA'I DBYINGS SU MNAL BAR DGONGS
TE,  RTA LO ZLA BA LNGA PA'I NYER LNGA'I NYIN SNYUN BBAS LCI
BA'I TSUL BSTAN SKABS,  DKA' CHEN SHES RAB DAR RGYAS SOGS GRVA
RIGS RNAMS KYIS,  RJE BLA MA NYID GAL TE GZHAN DU DGONGS

032 **,  ,PA GTAD PA DUS LA BBAS PA'I BSHOL DU MED PA YIN TSE,
ZHING 'DI'I BSTAN 'GRO'I DPAL DU SLAR YANG SPRUL PA'I SKU 'KHRUL
MED ZHEG MYUR DU PHEBS DGOS TSUL BA NAN TAN PHUL BAR ZHAL NAS
KHYED RANG

TSOS DKON MTSOG LA GSOL THOB,  NGAS KYANG DKON MCHOG LA GSOL BA
'DEBS ZHES PHEBS PAS DNGOS SU SPRUL SKU 'BYON PA'I ZHAL BZHES MA
GNANG YANG DON LA ZHAL GYIS BZHES PAR MDZOD DO, ,GSUNG 'DI TZAM
YANG BLO BROS DANG LDAN

PAS ZHIB TU BRTAGS NA GNAD CHE BAR SNANG STE,  ZHUS LAN NOR BU'I
PHRENG LAS,  RANG GI YON TAN SBA BYA ZHING, ,GZHAN GYI YON TAN
BSGRAG PAR BYA, ,ZHES DANG,  'JAM MGON SA PAn GYIS,  BLUN PO YON
TAN KHAR 'BYIN CING, ,MKHAS PA YON 

TAN KHONG DU SPED, ,CES GSUNGS PA LTAR,  RJE BLA MA NYID SKYE
'CHI LA DBANG THOB PA'I DAM PA KHYAD PAR CAN YIN PA RNAM THAR
MTHONG BA RNAMS KYIS SHES PA LTAR YIN KYANG,  DE LTA BU'I RNAM
PA MI DZAD PAR THUGS SHIN TU SGAM PA BKA' GDAMS GONG

MA'I RNAM THAR BDAG GIR BZHES TE BDE LEGS THAMS CAD KYI TZA BA
DKON MCHOG YIN PAS,  GRVA SLOB SPYIN BDAG SOGS DANG LDAN MTHA'
DAG GIS RANG 'DOD SPANGS TE GSOL BA RTZE GCIG TU BTAB NA,  DKON
MCHOG GI BYIN RLABS DANG THUGS RJE

'BA' ZHIG GI MTHU LAS NYI MA RANG SHAR BZHIN DU GSAL BAR 'GYUR RO, 
,ZHES 'DOMS PAR MDZAD PA GOR MA CHAG GO, ,DE NAS LUG LO ZLA BA
DANG PO'I TSES GNYIS KYI NYIN MDO SMAD KYI SDE CHEN PO DGON LUNG
BYAMS PA GLING GI SRUNG MA RTEN KHOG

TU SPYAN DRANGS PAR RJE DE NYID KYI SPRUL SKU 'BYON MIN GYI LUNG
BSTAN ZHUS PAR,  SRUNG MA NYID KYIS KHA DAR SRID ZHI BDE SKYID
MA RING BA ZHIG GI STEN DU RTAGS BRGYAD MA SER PO ZHIG DANG,
DE'I STEN DU NYIN BDE DKAR PO DRI MA MED PA RNAMS BRTZEGS TE ZHING

 RING THUNG SNYOMS PAR BSGRIGS PA DKA' 'CHEN ZHES RAB DAR RGYAS
LA GNANG NAS RTOG DPYOD GYIS ZHES ZHES PHEBS,  DE LA THAMS CAD
KYIS DPYAD PAS,  SPRUL SKU MI RING BAR 'BYON PA DANG,  BYON PA
NYID KYANG SKU TSE MDZAD 'PHRIN RGYAS PA

DANG, ,MDZAD 'PHRIN BZANG PO LA BRTAN NAS ZHI'I SKYID 'PHEL BA'I
BRDAM MTSON DU DPYAD PA PHYIS SU DE KHON BZHIN DU BYUNG 'DUG GO,
,CHU BZANG RIN PO BLO BZANG BSTAN PA'I RGYAL MTSAN LA SPRUL SKU
MYUR 'BYON GYI GSOL 'DE BAS ZHUS

PA BZHIN LJAGS RTZOM MDZAD SKABS,  BRKA SHES DGE MTSAN 'OD DKAR
SPROL BZHIN DU, ,THUB BSTAN KUNDA'I DPAL DU GSAL GYUR CIG, ,CES
GNANG BA DANG DUS MTSUNGS SU DGON LUNG GI TSOGS DUD 'BUD PA
'GRIG PAS SPRUL SKU NGES PAR

KHYOD RANG DANG BSOD

039 **, ,NAMS, TSE RING SGROL MA SOGS PHRAL DU PHYIR RANG YUL DU

BSKON TE BZUNG NAS

DKA' BCU BLO GROS DAR RGYAS BCAS CHIBS BSU BA MI NYUNG TZAM ZHIG

BRGYA PHRAG MANG POS PHYAG DBANG ZHUS PAR,  DRIGS ZHAN 'BRING

CHU 'DI LA KHRUS MI BYED,  LA PHA GI'I PHA ROL LAN RGYUG CHU CHE

GSAL POR GSUNGS PAS,  THAMS CA NGO 

SHING DER 'TSOGS RNAMS YID CHES KYI GNAS SU BKOD,  DE NAS RIM

RJES 'JUG LA, ,GDAMS PA STZAL BA RJES SU SGRUB BZHED NAS, ,MDA'
NA CHU BRAG 'THAB PAS GNAS SGO BSRUNGS, ,KHOR YUG NAGS KYI YOL
BAS MI MNGON

BSGRIBS, ,PHYOGS MTSAMS GCAN GZAN GTUM PO'I MEL TSE CAN, ,MA LA
YA 'DRA'I RI BO'I RTZER BYON TE, ,GNYIS PA'I GROGS NI GRIB MA
LAS MED CING, ,NYI ZLA'I 'CHAR NUB BLTA LAS SPROS GZHAN DOR,
,NYIN MO'I BZA'

BTUNG SPANGS PA'I DKA' THUB KYIS, ,MKHA' 'GRO PHUG RON RTZE BA'I
DOR 'GRIMS, ,'DI NI SKYES RABS DU MAR SPYANG YON LA, ,GOMS PA'I
RANG GI NGANG TSUL NGOM PA'AM, ,TING 'DZIN BDER SRED NAGS KYI
DRANG LA, ,CO

'DRI BYED CES BDAG YID 'PHYANG MO NYUG  ,KYE MA 'GRO MANG SROG
GI 'KHRI SHING NI, ,GYUL GYI SPU GRIS GCOD PAR GZAS PA YANG,
,GANG GI MTSAN TZAM MTHUN YIS PHYIR BZLOG PA, ,'DIS KYANG
MTSUNGS MED SKYABS SU CIS MI

RTOGS, ,SEMS CAN GZHAN LA PHAN PA'I DON 'GYUR NA, ,SPU GRIS BAR
MED GTAM PA'I LAM DU YANG, ,PAD MTSO MTHONG PA'I NGAN PA LTAR
'JUG PA, ,THUGS RJE'I DBANG GYUR KHYOD LA SKYABS SU MCHI, ,DE
NAS DMAG SGAR SU PHEBS

PAR NYE BA NA,  LCANG SKYA BLA BRANG GI PHYAG MDZOD BA YAN NANG
SO ZER BA NA RE,  DA NI SPRUL SKU RANG DBANG MED PAR DMAG NANG
DU PHEBS DGOS PA 'DUG  ,GRA PA'I KHROD NA PHYAG GYOG LA 'GRO
'DOD MKHAN YOD TSE SHIN TU LEGS,  GSOD SAR 'GRO

BA YIN GSHIS DANG BLANG GIS 'GRO MKHAN MA BYUNG NA TSAG RGYAG PA
DKA',  NGA RANG NI LO YANG RGAS PAS BLA MA GONG MA'I RTEN GSUM
DANG PHYAG BU YOD PA 'DI RNAMS BSRUNG NAS 'DUG PA LAS,  SPRUL
SKU'I RJES LA 'GRO RGYU MIN NO ZHES PAGS

PA SNGON PO'I LBA'I RANG SKAD BSGRAGS LA,  AA RTZE CHOS RJES
NGED RANG SPRUL SKU DGUNG LO BZHI'I DUS NAS DA LTA'I BAR 'BRAL
MED DU PHYAG GYOG BGYIS PA YIN, ,DA CHA GNAD 'GAG LA THUG DUS
BLOS GTOR MI PHOD PAS 'CHEN MNYAM 'CHI DANG,

GSON NAM NYAM GSON MIN PA MED ZER,  DE BZHIN DU GZHUNG BZANG
SNYING STOBS CHE BA'I GRA PA DGU TZAM GYIS PHYAG GYOG TU 'GRO BA
KHAS BLANGS,  DPON GYOG BCU GCIG PO RIM GYIS RGYA'I DMAG SGAR
YOD SAR 'BYOR,  GRA PA DGU PO NANG DU MA

BTANG BAR,  AA RTZE CHOS RJE GCIG PU SPRUL SKU RIN PO CHE DANG BCAS
YO'U CANG JUN GYI DRUNG KHRID PAS,  RAS GUR SHIN TU CHE BA ZHIG
GI DBUS NA KHRI MTHON PO STAG LPAGS KYI GDAN BTING BA ZHIG CANG
JUN KHOR RANG 'JIGS RDAM CHE BA'I TSUL

GYIS 'KHOD PA'I GYAS GYON DU DPON CHEN BRJID BAG CAN DU DANG
MTSON CHA SNA TSOGS ZANG ZING DU 'PHYAR BA GSHID MA'I NGAN TSUL
CAN MANG PO PHRING TSAR DU BSGRIGS PA RNAMS KYIS KU CO SGROGS PA
SOGS SHIN TU 'JIGS SHING SKYI GYA' BA'I

046 **, ,DBUS SU SKU RIN PO CHE ZHABS PUS BTZUGS NAS BZHUGS SU
BCUG  ,CANG JUN GYIS SKAD KYI NGA RO CHEN POS,  SPRUL SKU KHYOD
LCANG SKYA HU THOG THU'I SKU SKYE YIN NAM ZER BA LA,  SPRUL SKU
RIN PO CHES, LHA

DANG BLA MA TSAD LDAN RNAMS KYIS BLA MA DE'I SKYE BA YIN GSUNGS
PAS DE'I GOS SAR BSDAD PA YIN CES GSUNGS PA LA,  'O NA KHYOD
RANG GI SKYE BA SNGON MA DE LA ?GONG MA CHEN POS BSKYANGS BDAG
RKYEN TSAD MED GNANG BA YIN PA LA,  KHYOD RANG DA

CHA ?GONG MA CHEN POR NGO LOG PA'I RGYU MTSAN CI YIN ZER,  DE LA
SPRUL SKU RIN PO CHES,  NGED RANG BYIS PA LO BRGYAD ZHIG LA
RGYAL PO CHEN PO LA LOG PA'I DPYAD GZHI MI SEMS YOD SU ZHIG GIS
BYED CES GSUNGS PAS,  KHO PA DPON PO

GZHAN RNAMS LA BLTAS NAS NGO 'DZUM TZAM BYED CING,  KHYOD LO LOG
PA MIN NA RANG GNAS SU MI SDOD PAR NAGS KHROD DBEN PA BGROD DKA'
BA'I GNAS SU 'GRO BHA CI YIN ZER BA LA,  SROG MI GCES MKHAN SU
YANG MED PAS MI GSONG

MKHAN GYI DMAG DPUNG CHEN PO YONG GI 'DUG ZER BAS SKRAG NAS BROS
PA YIN ZHES GSUNGS PAR DPON PO THAMS CAD BZHAD GAD THEG GI BA
BYAS,  DE LTAR NYAM NGA BA DANG BAG TSA BA CUNG ZAD KYANG MED
PAR DRIGS PAS MYOS PA'I SKYE BO

KLAN KA 'TSOL BA DE'I SLOBS PA BCOM PAS,  KHYOD NGO LOG GNONG
STE GYOG ZHIG LA BRDA SPYAR NAS,  DES PHYI ROL TU THON CES SKROD
PA LTA BU BYED PA BZHIN,  RAS GUR GYI RA BA'I PHYI LOG TU PHEBS
PA NA ZHABS PHYI PA GZHAN RNAMS

SA LA 'GYEL ZHING MYA NGAN GYI CHO NGE 'DEBS KYI NA 'DUG PA
RNAMS KYIS SPRUL PA'I SKU NYAM NYES MED PAR PHEBS PA MTHONG NAS
DGA' SPRO'I SHUGS KYIS PHYAG ZHABS NA BZA' CI RIGS NAS 'CHANG STE
RE ZHIG GI BAR DU PHAN TSUN GTAM 'DRI BA YANG 

MI DRAN PAR LUS,  DE NAS BZHUGS GNAS RAS GUR ZHIG TU PHEBS PA
NA,  CANG JUN GYI MI ZHIG BTANG NAS GSOL CHAS PHRAN BU PHUL
ZHING,  SANG NYIN NAS DMAG SGAR 'DEGS PA DANG LHAN DU ZI LING DU
PHEBS DGOS,  GZHON PA DANG

CHAS KA RNAMS NYIN RE BZHIN SPROD PA YIN,  DPON CHUNG ZHIG DANG
DMAG MI KHA SHAS 'BRAL MED DU 'GRO RGYU YIN ZER,  SANG NYIN
NADS DMAG SGAR 'DEGS PA DANG LHAN DU TSA ZHAG GAR BBAS SU MNYAM
DU PHEBS,  SPRUL SKU RIN PO CHER NYIN

BZHIN CHIBS RTA RE BYUNG,  PHYAG GYOG PA RNAMS LA SKABS 'GA'
ZHIG TU ZHON STER KYANG DE MA THAG DMAG MI NGAN PA SOGS KYIS
'PHROG NAS RANG RANG GI RTA SGA KHUR NAS 'GRE DGOS PA DANG,
DSOL CHAS SOGS MDZOD NAS THON NA'ANG

BAR NAS GZHAN GYIS PHRI STE,  NGAN NGON NYUNG NGU TZAM RE LAS MA
BYUNG BAS DPON GYOG RNAMS SHIN TU 'O BRGYAL BA ZHIG LA ZI LING
MKHAR DU 'BYOR,  'DI YAN LA ?GONG MA'I BKA' BZANG PO PHEBS YOD
PA MA SHES PAS PHYAG GYOG PA

RNAMS NYIN RE BZHEN DE RING SKYON MA BYUNG YANG SANG NYIN CI
'DRA YONG SNYAM PA DANG LHAG PAR ZI LING DU SLEBS NAS GA 'DRA
BYAS YONG SNYAM SAMS NGAL 'BA' ZHIG GIS NYIN MTSAN 'DA' BAR
GYUR,  SPRUL SKU RIN PO CHE THUGS TSAB PA SOGS

047 **, ,KYI RNAM PA CUNG ZAD MED PAR MA ZAD,  RANG RE RNAMS
ZHAG KHA SHAS KYI BAR SRAN BTZUGS NA DE NAS BZA' BTUNG ZHIM PO
BZA' BA DANG LTAD MO YA MTSAN CAN MANG PO MTHONG RGYU YIN MOD
CES PHYAG GYOG PA

RNAMS LA DBUGS DBYUNG BA'I GSUNG YANG YANG PHEBS PAR PHYAG GYOG

BA 'DRA ZHES DGA' DGA' LTAR

BYED,  'GA' ZHIG GIS YA MTSAN RANG GA 'DRA YIN KYANG LTAD MO
SNGAR MA MTHONG BA ZHIG MTHONG DOGS 'DUG ZER,  ZI LING DU PHEBS
PA NA BZHUGS GNAS KYI KHANG PA SOGS GANG CI'I GRA BSGRIG GZAB
RGYAS 'DUG PA DANG MA 'GYANGS PAR

?GONG MA'I BKA' BZANG PO'I GSER YIG BSGRAGS PAS THAMS CAD KYI

LANG TSO LA 'GRAN PA BYANG,    ,DUS GSUM SHES BYA'I RI MO JI

'DI YI MKHYEN PA'I ME LONG DU, ,DSAL BAR BKRA YANG TSUR MTHONG

BZHIN MNGON SUM GYUR TSE GZOD DE DAG  ,YID CHES DAD PAS THAL MO

RIM GRO PHUN SUM

TSOGS PA BSGRUBS SHING,  SNGAR SOR PHYAG GYOG PA BCU LAS MED
KYANG,  DE NAS CHE PHRA MANG POS PHYAG GYOG LA HAB THOB KYIS JE
MANG DANG,  SNGAR GYI BA YAN NANG SO YANG SLEBS NAS PHYAG MDZOD
KYI GOS BYAS PA SOGS 'KHOR BA'I

MTSAN NYID MIG GIS MTHONG RGYU DANG LAG PAS 'DZIN RGYU YOD PA

DPON PO RNAMS KYIS RGYA'I SMAN PA NYAMS RGYUS YOD PA MANG PO'I
NGAG BSDUR GYIS SMAN DANG DBYAD 'JAM PO'I

RIGS RNAMS PHUL ZHING,  DSOL CHAS 'PHROD BSTEN SOGS GZAB PAR

SU ZHABS BRTAN RIM GRO RGYA CHER BSGRUB PAS CHER MA 'GYANGS PAR
ZLA BA BZLAS NAN TAN MDZAD DGOS

048 **, ,ZHI'I ZER BA'I ZLOS GAR GZIGS MO PHUL,  DE DUS MDO SMAD

DU BZHUGS,  RJE THU'U BKVAN RIN PO CHE DUS SKABS DER PE'I CING

049 **, ,MDZAD TSUL NAN TAN GYIS 'DIBS PHUL,  SKABS SHIG GONG MA

YE SGES DGAN DRANGS NAS YUN RIN POR BZHUGS PA'I GTZUG LAG KHANG

051 **, ,RAB DGA' MJUG MA BKRAM PA'I ZLOS GAR BZHIN, ,GANG SKU

SPAS GSANG GANG DRAG GIS SDOD DGOS BYUNG BA LA,  RJE THU'U BKVAN

DANG,  SPRUL SKU RIN PO CHE NAS KYANG ZUR 'DEGS MDZAD DE ?GONG
MAR ZHU MKHAS KYI SGO NAS,  DGON LUNG PA RNAMS RI KHROD GSUM
DANG,  GSER KHOG PA RNAMS PHUN TSOGS LUNG PA'I RI KHROD DU BSDAD
CHOG PA BYUNG,  LO KHA

SHAS KYI BAR DE LTAR LA,  SLAR YANG GONG MA CHEN POR THABS MKHAS
KYI ZHU BA DANG MDZAD SGO GANG ZAB GNANG BAR BRTEN,  DGON PA
GNYIS KAS SNGAR GYI RANG RANG GI GNAS GZHI BDAG GIR BYAS CHOG PA
BYUNG ZHING,  GTZUG LAG KHANG

DANG GRVA KHANG RNAMS KYANG ?GONG MA'I MDZOD NAS GSAR BSKRUN
DANG,  LHA SDE RNAMS RGYA 'OG TU TSUD PA PHYIR MA SPRAD KYANG,
DE'I TSAB TU LO RE BZHIN MDZOD NAS PHOG GTAN 'JAGS SU GNANG BA
BCAS ZHU DON SMIN RGYAS BYUNG,  DE NAS DGUNG

LO BCO BRGYAD LA PHEBS KYI BAR DU RGYAN DRUG MCHOG GNYIS KYI
GZHUNG LA SPYANGS PA GTZO BOR MDZAD CING ZHAR LA CHOS BKA' CI
RIGS KYANG GSAN PAR MDZAD SNANG BA LA LO TSIGS KYI NGES PA SA
BON MA BYUNG BAS 'BRI BAR MA SPOBS PAS

PHYOG GCIG TU 'GOD PAR BYA STE,  DE YANG SLOB MA'I THA SHAL BA
BDAG GIS RJE BLA MA NYID KYI RNAM PAR THAR PA YI GER BKOD PA
ZHIG THUGS RJES GZIGS DGOS TSUL YANG YANG ZHUS PAR GSUNG LAS,
DENG SANG GZHUNG LUGS MANG PO LA

THOS BAS MRGYA CHEN PO BYAS PAR RLOM PA PHAL CHE BA ZHIG NI,
KHO 'DI ZER NA NGA 'DI ZER GYI SHAG 'GYID PA TZAM GTZO BOR BYAS
TE,  MI TSE HRIL GYIS THAL PHRENG NYOG PO ZHIG KHO NA LA MGO
'GAS 'GAS SU RTZOD PA LAS,  GZHUNG LUGS CHEN MO RNAMS

GO BA DBYIS PHYIN PA 'TSAL MKHAN NYIN MO'I SKAR MA BZHIN DU DKON
PAR SNANG,  DE DGAL BLTAS NA,  KHO BO MTSAN NYID KYI GRVA SAR
ZHUGS NAS SLOB GNYER BYED PA MA BYUNG NA'ANG,  SHING RTA CHEN PO
RNAMS KYI GZHUNG LUGS DUM DANG RJE YAB SRAS KYI

052 **, ,LEGS BSHAD RNAMS LA BLO GROS ZHIB MOS THOS BSAM BYED
LUGS TSAD DANG LDAN PA,  RJE BLA MAS RANG KYI RTOGS BRJOD 'DUN
LEGS MAR GSUNGS PA DANG CHA 'DRA BTZAM ZHIG BGYIS PAS

DA CHA GZHUNG LUGS DE RNAMS LA GO BA PHYOGS 'GRO ZHIG CHAGS PA'I
LUGS YIN,  'DI KHO BO LA LTOS PA'I RNAM THAR BZANG SHOS SHIG YIN
SNYAM PA YOD,  DE LAS GZHAN SONG BSDAD BYAS PA THAMS CAD THAR DU
BYED NA MI THAMS      

CAD LA RNAM THAR PO TI CHE BA RE YONG 'GRO ZHES PHEBS PAR,  BDAG
GIS 'ON RJE BLA MA NYID NAS MDO SNGAGS KYI GZHUNG LUGS CHEN MO
RNAMS LA THOS BSAM JI LTAR MDZAD TSUL DE RNAMS YI GER BKOD PA
ZHIG CIS KYANG THUGS RJES GZIGS

DGOS ZHUS PAR,  YI GER BKOD PA'I DGOS PA MED KHYOD DE TZAM DO
GAL CHEN NGAS NGAG LAM NAS BSHAD KYI GSUNGS NAS,  SKUN PHRA MO'I
GNAS SKABS SU MDO PHYOGS KYI THUGS GNYER GTZO BOR MDZAD TSUL
DANG,  DUS DE DANG PHYIS SU RGYAL

DBANG DANG KHRI CHEN GYI ZHABS LA GTUGS NAS MDO SNGAGS SPYI DANG
KHYAD PAR DU RGYUD KYI RGYAL PO DPAL GSANG BA 'DUS PA DANG 'KHOR
LO MCHOG GNYIS KYI SKOR LA THOS BSAM GYIS BDAR SHA BCAD TSUL
RTOGS BRJOD 'DUN LEGS MA

DANG SPYAR TE ZHIB RGYAS SHIG THUGS BRTZE BAS 'DOMS PAR MDZAD PA
SHIN TU NGO MTSAR BA 'DUG NA'ANG,  BDAG BLO GROS DMAN PAS GSUNG
BSHAD MTHA' DAG JI LTA BA BZHIN BLO LA 'DZIN THUB PA MA BYUNG
ZHING,  DBYIBS TZAM ZHIG YID

YUL DU NGES PAR BGYIS PA RNAMS 'DIR BRJOD PAR BYA STE,  DE YANG
THAR 'DOD RNAMS KYI 'JUG NGOGS NI RGYAL PA'I BSTAN PA RIN PO CHE
KHO NA YIN CING,  BSTAN PA LA 'JUG PA'I RIM PA YANG MDZOD LAS,
TSUL GNAS THOS DANG

SAM LDAN PAS, ,SGOM PA LA NI RAB TU SPYOR, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR
GZHI TSUL KHRIMS RNAMS PAR DAG PA LA GNAS NAS THOS BSAM SGOM
GSUM GYI RIM PAS 'JUGS LAS 'JUG TSUL GZHAN MED CING,  DE LAS
THOG MAR THOS PA RGYA

CHEN PO DGOS PA NI, RJE THAMS CAD MKHYEN PAS,  BLANG DOR GNAS LA
KUN NAS 'THOM PA'I MUN, ,YANG DAG THOS PA'I SGRON MES MA BSAL
BAR, ,LAM MI SHES NA THAR PA'I GRONG MCHOG TU, ,'JUG PAR 'GYUR
BA SMOS KYANG CI ZHIG

DGOS, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR RO, ,DENG DUS KYI DAM PA'I SKYE BAR
KHAS 'CHEB PHAL MO CHE NI,  RJE BLA MA NYID KYI GSUNG LAS,  BYIS
PA'I DUS NAS THOS BSAM LONG MED PAR, ,DAR GOS KYIS KLUBS TSONG
ZONG BZHIN DU 'GRIM, ,DAD

GSHIN DKOR GYI ZAS LA BAG MED SPYOD, ,GNAS BRTAN DGE 'DUN PHYAG
DANG BSNYEN BKUR LEN, ,LNGA BDO'I SKU SKYE RNAMS LA THUGS RJES
GZIGS, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA DANG,  RGYAL DBANG LNGA PA CHEN POS,  MI
SHES GDOL PA'I PHRUG GU DAR

ZAB KYIS, ,PHANG PHUNG MDZES PAR BYAS TE MTHON PO'I KHRIR, ,BLUN
PO'I 'KHOR TSOGS DBUS NA 'GYINGS PA YI, ,BA MOS THUB BSTAN PAD
TSAL 'JOMS KYIS DOGS, ,ZHES GANG GSUNGS PA'I NGANG TSUL LAS MA
'DAS NA'ANG,   
   
053 **,  ,BDAG CAG GI DPAL LDAN BLA MA 'DI NYID KYIS SPYOD TSUL
DE LTA BU NGAN SKYUGS KYI PHUNG PO LTAR GZIGS NAS BYON GYI MKHAS
GRUB TSAD LDAN RNAM PAR THAR PA DANG RJES SUM THUN PAR

SKU NA PHRA BA'I GNAS SKABS 'DIR GZHUNG LUGS RGYA CHEN PO RNAMS
THOS BSAM GYIS GTAN LA 'BEBS PA LA THUGS GZHOL BAR MDZAD DO, ,DE
YANG THOG MAR MTSAN NYID PO TI LNGA LA SBYANGS LA MTHAR PHYIN
CING,  RJE GONG MA'I ZHABS

PHYIR RGYUN RING BZHUGS NAS MNGO SNGAGS KYI GSAN PA RGYA CHEN PO
MDZAD PA DANG MNYES PA GSUM GYI SGO NAS RJE DE KYI THUGS LA
BTAGS PA'I GRVA SLOB THUN MONG MA YIN PA BZANG SHU DKA' CHEN
SHES RAB DAR RGYAS SAM NGAG DBANG

CHOS LDAN ZHES BYA BA LUNG RIGS KYI DBANG PHYUG CHEN PO DE NYID

PAS RTZOL BA CHER MA DGOS RIGS LAM SHIN TU PHRA BA RNAMS THUGS
SU CHUD,  DKA' CHEN

NAS THOG MAR RJE GONG MA'I GSUNG 'BUM DU BZHUGS PA'I RTZA BA'I

LUNG KHRID 'BUL BAR MDZAD CING,  DE NAS BZUNG THUGS NYAMS SU
BZHES PAR LHA'I RNAM PA LA GSAL

SNANG KHYAD PAR CAN THON PAS SNANG BA THAMS CAD RJE BTZUN GYI

LAM SHAR NAS THUGS LA CUNG ZAD MI BDE BA LTA BU BYUNG,  PHYIS SU
DGUNG LO MTHON POR PHEBS SKABS,  DE

DUS DE LTAR BYUNG BA BZHIN DA CHA YANG SKABS 'GA' ZHIG TU 'DRA'I

GSUNGS,  'DI NI NGES PA'I DON DU RJE BLA MA NYID KYI GZIGS NGOR
THA MAL GYI SNANG BA 'CHAR MI SRID PAS

SHAR MCHOG GI SNANG BA LAS 'OS MED KYANG,  THUN MONG GI SNANG

CHAGS RTZOL MED DU SHAR BA DGON MI

ZA'O,           ,THOS PA'I SGRON MES RMONGS MUN MA BAS LAN, ,LAM

KHYOD KYIS SPIL, ,DE TSE

054 **, ,MI PHAM CHOS RJE DANG, ,'DZAM GLING RGYAN DRUG MCHOG

'GREL GZHAN THAMS CAD DANG,  RJE BLA MA'I LEGS BSHAD GSER GYI

PA LA MKHAS PA'I GO

PHANG BRNYES PAR GYUR TO, ,BYAMS CHOS PHYI MA RNAMS LAS MDO SDE

'GREL PA CI RIGS PA LA BRTEN NAS TSIG DON MA LUS PA THUGS SU

MDZOD LAS, ,MI PHAM MGON GYIS NYER BLANGS NOR BU'I TSOGS, ,DNGOS

GYI RIM PAR BSGRIGS MKHAS PA, ,DENGS DUS NA KHYOD NYID GCIG PU

055 **, ,tIK THAR LAM DSAL BYED GNYIS THUGS 'DZIN MDZAD CING,

TSUL SOGS BSHAD YAM TZAM MA YIN PA'I GO BA GTING TSUGS PA 'KHRUNGS,

056 **, ,NA,  THOS MA BYAS LA RNAMS LTA CI GZHUNG LUGS MANG DU

057 **, ,RGYUN LDAN MDZAD PAS,  NUB CIG MNAL LAM DU,  RJE NGAG

ZHAL BYANG PHYOGS SU GZIGS TE,  BZHENGS STABS SU BZHUGS PA'I

BA GDAB DGOS,  KHYED RANG RJE BTZUN 'JAM PA'I DBYANGS SPYI BOR
