PA DANG,  MGON PO SRUNG MA'I GTZO BOR MDZAD NA ?'JAM DBYANGS
GONG MA'I DBU BLAR GYUR NAS,  SKU TSE

DANG BSOD NAMS GONG 'PHEL YONG BA'I PHYIS 'BYUNG GI BRDA MTSON
DU MNGON ZHING,  SNGA PHYI GNYIS NI 'OG TU 'BYUNG BA BZHIN BLA
MA 'JAM PA'I DBYANGS KYIS RJES SU BZUNG STE,  ZAB MO DBU MA'I
LTA BA THUGS RGYUD LA 'KHRUNGS PA'I LTAS SU

GOR MA CHAGS SO, ,GONG GI MNAL LAM DE DAG NI PHYAG BRIS KYI
SHOG DRIL NGO MA MTHONG BA LTAR BRIS PA YIN NO, ,DE NAS RING PO
MA LON PA NA NUB CIG MNAL LAM DU,  AA MDO BLA RGAN YIN ZER BA'I
AA TZA RA ZHIG RJE NYID KYI GZIM

PHUGS SU KHRI ZHIG GI KHAR 'KHOD NAS PI LBA ZHIG BRDUNG GI 'DUG
PA GSAN PAS,  DE'I SGRA LAS RTEN 'BREL BSTOD PA'I TSEGS YONGS SU
RJOGS PA GSAL BAR THON PA ZHIG RMIS,  DE NAS ZAB MO DBU MA'I LTA
BA KHYAD PAR CAN THUGS

058 **,  ,RGYUD LA 'KHRUNGS PA YIN PAR SNANG,  'DI NI RJE BLA MA
DKON MCHOG MTSAN CAN LA ZHAL NAS DNGOS SU GSUNGS 'DUG CING,  RJE
DE NYID KYIS GSUNG CHOS 'GA' SKABS SU LCANG SKYA THAMS

CAD MKHYEN PAS DBU MA'I LTA BA THOG MAR RNYED PA DGUNG LO BCU
GSUM DUS YIN PA 'DUG, ,DE DUS MNAL LTAS KYANG GONG GI DE 'DRA
BYUNG BA SNANG ZHES GSUNGS SHING BSNGAGS BRJOD MDZAD PA THOS SO,
,'DI NI MGON PO KLU SGRUB DANG

RJE BLA MA NGO BO GCIG PA'I RNAM 'PHRUL KYIS PI WAm GI DPES DES
DON ZAB MO 'DOMS PAR MDZAD PA BSAM GYIS MI KHYAB PA'I RNAM PAR
THAR PA'O,,          ,RDZUN PA RMI LAM GRONG KHYER NA, ,RDZUN PA
SMRA BA'I SLOB DPON

GYIS, ,RDZUN PA LAS KYANG RDZUN PA'I GLUS, ,RDZUN PA'I CHOS KYI
DON BSTON PAS, ,SGOM RGYU MED PA'I DON BSGOM PAS, ,GROL RGYU MED
PA'I 'PHRANG GROL NAS, ,THOB RGYU MED PA'I 'BRAS THOB PA'I, ,LTA
RGYU MED PA'I LTA BA RNYED, ,BDEN PA BTZAL

BAS RDZUN PA MTHONG, RDZUN PA MTHONG BAS BDEN PA RNYED, ,BDEN
RDZUN MNYAM NYID GZIGS MO LA, ,MNYAM RJES MED PAR YENGS 'DI
RMAD,       ,'DI DUS YIN NAM DBU MA LA 'JUG PA'I RNAM BSHAD SEMS
BSKYED DANG PO YAN

CHAD CIG LJAGS RTZOM MDZAD 'DUG PA LUNG RIGS KYI MTHA' CHOD CING
BLO GROS DANG LDAN PA RNAMS LA GO BA BDE BLAG TU STER BAR BYED
PA'I LEGS BSHAD KYI GTER CHEN POR 'DUG GO, ,GZHAN YANG MDO KUN
LAS BTUS DANG RIGS TSOG

LHAG MA LNGA,  BSTOD TSOGS,  BZHI BRGYA PA RTZA 'GREL,  SPYONG
'JUG RTZA 'GREL,  BSLAB PA KUN LAS BTUS,  DBU MA RGYAN DANG,
DBU MA SNANG BA,  SGOM RIM GSUM SOGS KLU SGRUB YAB SRAS KYI
GZHUNG GANG YOD THAMS CAD LA THOS BSAM

DPYIS PHYIN PA MDZAD,  ZHAL NAS,  RTZA 'JUG GI DON LA GO BA
DPYIS PA RNYED PHYIN,  GZHAN RNAMS PHAL CHER DE'I YAN LAG LTA
BUR SNANG BAS NGAL BA BDE TZAM MI DGOS PA CES GSUNGS,  'DI DUS
DRANG NGES RNAM 'BYED LEGS

BSHAD SNYING PO TSANG MA THUGS LA BZUNG ZHING DKA' BA'I GNAS LAM
MKHAS PA RNAMS DANG 'BEL GTAM MANG DU MDZAD PAS DBU SEMS KYI
MKHAS PA SO SO'I RIGS 'GROS PHRA RNAMS MA 'DRES PAR THUGS SU
CHUD,  ZHAL NAS,  LEGS BSHAD

SNYING BO'I DKA' 'GREL THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA DGE 'DUN RGYA MTSO
DANG GNYAL STON DPAL 'BYOR LHUN GRUB KYIS MDZAD PA GNYIS KYANG
SHIN TU LEGS SNANG MOD,  DA DUNG YANG DKA' PA'I GNAD DPYIS PHYIN
PAR BSHAD DGOS PA 'GA' ZHIG YOD

'DUG PAS,  DKA' 'GREL ZHIG RTZOM 'DUN GYIS LEGS BSHAD SNYING
PO'I GZHUNG TSIG 'GA' ZHIG LA MCHAN BU BTAB PA YIN KYANG SKABS
SHIG DRIL RNAMS BOR NAS MA RNYED PA LA,  DUS PHYIS GZHAN ZHIG GI
NGAG RTZOM GRAS SU BCUG

'DUG CES GSUNGS NAS BZHAD MO MDZAD,  DBU MA'I SKOR LA THUGS
GNYER GNANG SKABS 'DI HA CANG THUGS BRTZON CHE BAS MTSAN MO YANG
ZHAL 'DON SKABS MA GTOGS PHAL CHER DPE GZIGS KHO NA MDZAD,
SKABS 'GA' ZHIG TU GCIG

059 **, ,BUR BZHUGS DUS BZHAD MO YUN RING GNANG BAR,  PHYAG
GYOGS PA TSOS HA CANG DPE GZIGS LA SGRIM DRAGS PAS THUGS RLUNG
GI RNAM PA YIN 'DRA BAS ZAD LHOR TZAM MDZAD NA LEGS SAM ZHUS

,  DE 'DRA MA YIN RGYA GAR KHA SPU CAN GYI RIGS PA 'GA' ZHIG LA
YA MCHEN SKYES NAS GAD MO SHOR BA YIN,  KHYOD TSO SEMS MI BDE BA
MI DGOS GSUNGS,  RTEN 'GREL BSTOD PA YANG YANG ZHAL 'DON MDZAD
CING DGOS PA KHYAD

PAR CAN ZHIG LA DGONGS NAS,  THUB PA'I DBANG PO DANG KLU SGRUB YAB
SRAS,  RGYAL BA TZONG KHA PA RNAMS KYI SKU BRNYAN RE YANG
BZHENGS PA MDZAD,  'DI DAG NI RJE BLA MAS,  DE TSE RING NAS
NYAMS PA'I RTOGS DKA'I GNAS, ,GANG GIS

BTZAL NAS RNYED PA'I RIGS PA'I LAM, ,'DI YI RNAM 'PHRUL CI LTA
BU ZHIG CES, ,GCIG PUR GNAS KYANG DGA' BA'I CA CO 'CHOR, ,ZHES
GSUNGS PA DANG,  RES 'GA' RGYAL LA DMIGS PA'I DAD PA DANG,
,SKABS 'GAR SHING RTA CHEN

SKU DRIN DRAN, ,GZHAN TSE DGE BA'I BSHES LA GUS PA DANG, ,MAR
GYUR 'GROL LA SNYING NAS BRTZE BA RNAMS, ,'DI DAG PHAN TSUN
'GRAN PA BZHIN DU 'PHEL, ,ZHES GANG GSUNGS PA LTAR THUGS RGYUR
LA CHOS KYI RO'I DGA' BA LHAG PAR 'PHEL

ZHING,   BCOM LDAN 'DAS LA TSAD MAS DRANGS PA'I DAD PA DANG,
SHING RTA CHEN PO RNAMS KYI SKU DRIN DRAN PA DANG,  SEMS CAN LA
BCOS MIN GYI SNYING RJE RNAMS 'GRAN PA BZHIN 'PHEL BA SHIN TU YA
MTSAN PA'I RNAM PAR THAR PA'O,             ,

THUB DBANG GANGS KYI RI BO LAS 'ONGS PA'I,  ,STONG NYID ZAB MO'I
GTAM GYI NYAL 'GRO'I RGYUN, ,KLU SGRUB YAB SRAS THUGS MTSOR
BZUNG BA GANG, ,KHYOD KYI RNAM DPYOD ZHAL DU RDZOGS PAR DSOL,
,MTHA' BRGYAD LTA BA NGAN PA'I RANG RONG BRAG

RIGS TSUL RDO RJES PHI MAR BSNYIL BYAS TE, ,SNANG STONG ZUNG
'JUG DBU MA'I LAM YANGS POR, ,RTEN 'BREL SGYU MA'I ROL GAR CIR
YANG BSGYUR, ,DE TSE CHU GTER CHEN PO'I KLONG, ,SHUGS DRAG 'BAB
CHUS GANG BA BZHIN, ,GANG GI THUGS NI

SPRO DGA' YI, ,RLABS PHRENG MCHOG TU GYO BAR GYUR, ,RANG BZHIN
MED LA BYA BYED BCING GROL KUN, ,BTAGS TZAM 'THAD PA DBU MA'I
GSANG TSIG NI, ,RIGS SMRA PHAL CHER NI TZO LTAR 'DON KYANG, ,JI
BZHIN GZIGS SHING GSUNG BA BYOD NYID

TZAM, ,DENG DUS 'THAD DANG MI 'THAD SGRUB PA DAG, ,PHAL CHER
'GRO BA BZHI YID BANG GIS TE, ,KHYOD NI RTON PA BZHI YIS DRANG
NGES DON, ,PHYE STE NGES PA'I DON LA 'JUG PAR MDZAD, ,SE MA KLU            
SGRUB YAB SRAS DGONGS PA'I MTHIL, ,BLO BZANG 

RGYAL BAS DSAL BAR PHE BA'I SROL, ,KHYOD 'BA'  ZHIG GI DRIN LAS
DUS 'DIR YANG, ,SKAL BZANG 'GA' LA BDUD RTZI'I DGA' STON GYUR,
,SLOB DPON PHYOGS GLANG YAB SRAS KYI GZHUNG LA THOS BSAM MDZAD
TSUL YANG,   'DUN LEGS

MA LAS,  ,BYAD PAR TSU ROL MTHONG BAS DNGOS PO YI, ,DE NYID GTAN
LA 'BEBS PA'I SGO GCIG PU, ,YANG DAG RIGS PA'I GZHUNG GI DKA'
GNAS LA, ,'BAD PA DU MAS YANG DANG YANG DU SPYANGS, ,ZHES GSUNGS
PA LTAR MDZAD DE,  DPAL

060 **, ,CHOS KYI GRAGS PA'I TSAD MA RNAM 'GREL GYI RTZA BA DANG
RGYAL TSAB RJE'I RNAM BSHAD THAR LAM GSAL BYED TSANG MA THUGS
'DZIN GNANG ZHING,  LHA SH'AKA RGYAN GSUM GYI RNAM 'GREL GYI
'GREL PA DANG,  BOD

KYI SA SKYA'I MKHAS PA RNAMS KYIS MDZAD PA'I RNAM 'GREL SKOR
MANG PO DANG,  LHAG PAR RIGS MDZOD RJE THAMS CAD MKHYEN PAS
KYANG GZIGS NAS THUGS 'PHROG TSUL RNAM THAR DU GSUNGS PAS, RIGS
MDZOD KYI DPE RTZOL BAS 'TSOL

BA GNANG STE GZIGS RTOG ZHIB TU MDZAD,  RNAM NGES DANG RIGS
THIGS DAR tIK GNYIS DANG,  MKHAS GRUNG RJE'I tIK CHEN DANG,  SDE
BDUN RGYAN,  RJE DGE 'DUN GRUB KYI RIGS RGYAN SOGS RANG PHYOGS
KYI YIG CHA GANG YOD RNAMS LA GZHAN

DRING MI 'JOG PA'I MKHYEN RAB KYIS RTOG DPYOD YANG DAG PA MDZAD,
 RNAM 'GREL SMON tIK DE DUS ZHIB TU BLTAS PAS SEMS LA PHAN PA
ZHIG BYUNG ZHES PHYES SU GSUNGS PA THOS,  DENG SANG TSAD MA'I
GZHUNG GI BSDUS TSAN ZUR BKOL KHA

SHAS RE LA RTAGS GSAL LA BYANG BAS RNAM 'GREL SHES PAR RLOM PA
RNAMS DANG MI 'DRA BAR RNAM 'GREL LE'U GNYIS PA'I SKABS SU LAM
DANG 'BRAS BU'I RNAM BZHAG GTAN LA PHAB PA DANG,  DE NYID LE'U
DANG POR RIGS PA YANG DAG

GIS JI LTAR SGRUB PA'I TSUL DANG,  LE'U GSUM PAR CHOS KYI BDAG
RGYAS PAR GTAN LA PHAB PA DANG,  LE'U BZHI PAR SNGAR LE'U GNYIS
PA DANG GSUM PAR DTHEG PA CHE CHUNG GI LAM GTAN LA PHAB PA RNAMS
RNAG GIS JI LTAR RTOGS

PA BZHIN DU DON DE NYID GZHAN LA BSTAN NAS RJES SU 'DZIN PA'I
TSUL DANG BCAS BSHAD RNAMS JI LTA BA BZHIN THUGS LA CHUD PAS
DPAL LDAN CHOS KYI GRAGS PA'I GZHUNG 'DI NYID THAR 'DOD RNAMS
KYI MIG GCIG PU LTA BUR RES PA GTING TSUGS

PA RNYED PAR GYUR TO,       ,RIGS PA'I DBANG PHYUG ZHAL SGO LAS
SKYUGS PA'I, ,RNAM DAG RIGS TSUL LA GSUM 'BAB PA'I RGYUN, ,TSIG
DON BRGYAN KYI YAN LAG YONGS RDZOGS PA, ,KHYOD THUGS GSER LDAN
LTO BAR RDZOGS PAR

'KHYIL, ,RTOG GE'I CHANG GIS CHES CHER MYOS PA YI, ,RNAM DPYOD
GNYIS 'THUNG SNA YI 'KHRI SHING RTZER, ,SGRUB DANG SUN 'BYIN
'KHOR LOG YO BA DES, ,SMRA BA DAN PA'I DPUNG TSOGS PHYE MAR
BRLAG  ,TSUL GSUM RTAGS KYI SPRIN PHUNG LAS BBAS

PA'I, ,DNGOS STOB RIGS PA'I THOG GIS SGRO SKUR BRAG  ,BSHIG DANG
LHAN CIG RIGS LAM GRU CHAR GYIS, ,THAR 'DOD SHING PA'I TSOGS LA
DGA' STON BSKRUN,     ,MCHOG GNYIS SU GRAGS PA YON SH'AKA GNYIS
KYI GZHUNG LA THOS

BSAN MDZAD TSUL NI,  SLOB DPON YON TAN 'OD KYI 'DUL BA MDO RTZA
BA TSANG MA THUGS 'DZIN MDZAD,  DE'I RGYA CHER 'GREL PA CHOS
BSHES KYIS MDZAD PA,   SH'AKYA 'OD KYI SUM BRGYA PA DANG 'OD
LDAN BCAS RGYA GZHUNG RNAMS DANG,   BOD 'GREL

THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA DGE 'DUN GRUB KYI GLING 'BUM DANG,  'DUL tIK
RIN CHEN 'PHRENG BA,  'DUL 'DZIN GYI BSLAB BYA CHEN MO,  GRVA
TSANG SO SO'I 'DUL BA'I YIG CHA GANG YOD ZHIB GZIGS DANG,  KHYAD
PAR DU KUN MKHYEN MTSO SNA

061 **,  ,PA'I 'DUL tIK NYI MA'I 'OD ZER GYI TSIG DON MTHA' DAG
THUGS SU CHUD MDZAD,  ZHAL NAS,   MTSO 'DUL 'DI BSHAD YAM TZAM
MA YIN PAR 'DUL BA LAM RIM GYI NYAMS LEN DANG SBYANG NAS

BSHAD 'DUG PAS,  'DUL BA RTZOD PAR 'KHYER BA TSO'I THUGS LA 'BAB
MIN JI LTAR YANG,  LAG LEN DU BTAB NAS SEMS 'DUL BA'I THABS SU
BYED MKHAN LA SHIN TU PHAN PA ZHIG 'DUG CES GSUNGS,  'DUL BA'I

LA PHYIS SU DGUNG LO MTHON POR PHEBS NAS KYANG GZIGS RTOG RGYUN
DU MDZAD CING,  'DUL ZHUNG CHA TSANG LA SDUM BDE BA ZHIG RGYUN
DU BLTA RTOG BYED PAR MKHO BA 'DUG GSUNGS NAS SNAR THANG PA NAM
MKHA' SHES RAB KYIS

MDZAD PA'I 'DUL BA'I BSTAN CHOS NOR BU'I 'PHRENG BA DGE SLONG GI
RGYAN ZHES PA DE GZIGS DPE CHED GNYIR DU BRIS TE GAR PHEBS SU
'BRAL SPANGS LTA BU MDZAD,  YON TAN THAMS CAD KYI GZHI MA SANGS
RGYAS KYI BSTAN PA'I NANG

MDZOD CHOS 'DUL BA LA NAN DE LTA BU MDZAD PA 'DI NI RNAM PAR
THAR PA MCHOG TU SHES PAR BYA'O,       ,DGAG SGRUB GNANG GSUM
RLABS PHRENG ROL PA CAN, ,'DUL LUNG 'BUM SNGE'I CHU GTER CHEN
POR DER, ,

BSHAD SGRUB GSER GYI GRU YIS LEGS ZHUGS NAS, ,RNAM GROL NOR BU
DED DPON KHYOD KYIS BLANGS, ,BSTAN PA'I NANG MDZOD DAM MA CHOS
'DUL BA NYID, ,GCES PAR DGONGS TE YI GLEGS BAM KYANG, ,CHOS GOS

BZHIN DU 'BRAL SPANGS MDZAD PA 'DI, ,BSTAN PA THUGS LA BRNGA
PA'I RNAM THAR TE, ,RANG NYID THUB PA'I RJES SU ZHUGS RLOM NAS,
,DE YI BCAS PA 'BAD PAS KHYAD GSOD CING, ,GZHAN TSUL DER NAN
GYIS SPYOR BYED PA, ,DE DAG BDE

GSHEGS BSTAN PA'I CHOM RKUN NO, ,KVA YI RNAG LA SNYING BRTE LDAN
PA DAG  ,BDUD KYI DBANG GYUR LOG PA'I BSHES GNYEN GYI, ,NGAN
SPYOD THA CHAD RJES SU MA 'BRANGS PAR, ,DAM PA'I RNAM THAR JI
BZHIN BSLAB PAR 'TSAL,     ,DE

LTAR RGYAN DRUNG MCHOG GNYIS RJES 'BRANG DANG BCAS PA'I GZHUNG
RNAMS LA PHYOGS RE BA DANG RAGS PA RES TSEM PAR MA BYAS PAR KUN
LA ZHIB TU SPYANGS PA RJE BLA MA TZONG KHA PA'I RNAM PAR THAR PA
PHYAG LEN DU THEBS PA 'DI LTA BU BDAG

CAG GI DPAL LDAN BLA MA 'DI NYID TZAM MA GTOGS,  NGUS PHYIS KYI
'GRO 'DREN DU KAHS 'CHE BA RNAMS DANG,  THOS PA RGYA CHEN PO
BYAS PAR RLOM PA RNAMS KYI KHYOD DU RE RE TZAM YANG MI SNANG
BAS,  TSUL 'DI NI GZHAN GYIS BRKUN DU

MED PA'I RNAM THAR DU BLO GROS DANG LDAN PA RNAMS KYIS SHES PAR
BYOS SHIG  ,GZHUNG CHEN MO DE DAG GI KHROD NAS KYANG DBU MA'I
SKOR LA 'BUR DU DOD PA'I THUGS GNYER NAN TAN MDZAD CING,  DE
SKOR KYI 'BEL GTAM LA YANG THUGS

SHIN TU DGYES PA ZHIG YOD DE,  'DI YANG RJE BLA MAS,  'DZAM
GLING MKHAS PA'I RGYAN GYUR 'DI RNAMS KYI, ,LEGS BSHAD KUN LA
SNYING NAS GUS MOS KYANG, ,'KHOR 'DAS RTEN 'BYUNG MI BSLU'I GTAN
TSIGS KYIS, ,MTHAR

062 **, ,'DZIN DMIGS GTAN THAMS CAD 'JIG BYED PA, ,ZLA BA LAS
'ONGS LEGS BSHAD 'OD DKAR GYIS, ,BLO MIG KUNNGA'I TSAL RAB PHYE
BA'I TSE, ,SANGS RGYAS BSKYANGS KYIS BSTAN PA'I LAM MTHONG

NAS, ,KLU SGRUB LUGS BZANG GTZO BOR 'DZIN SU, ,ZHES DANG,  RTEN
'BREL BSTONG PA LAS,  KHYOD KYIS BLA MED THEG PA'I TSUL, ,YOD
DANG MED PA'I MTHA' SPANGS TE, ,JI BZHIN 'GREL BAR LUNG BSTAN
PA, ,KLU SGRUB GZHUNG

LUGS KUNNGA'I TSAL, ,DRI MED 'BYED PA'I DKYIL 'KHOR RGYAS,
,GSUNG RAB MKHA' LA THOGS MED RGYU, ,MTHAR 'DZIN SNYING GI MUN
PA SEL, ,LOG SMRA'I RGYU SKAR ZIL GNON PA, ,DPAL LDAN ZLA BA'I
LEGS BSHAD KYI, ,'OD DKAR

'PHRENG PAS GSAL BYAS PA, ,BLA MA'I DRIN GYIS MTHONG BA'I TSE,
,BDAG GI YID KYI NGAL BSO THOB, ,CES GSUNGS PA DANG TSUL MTHUNG
PA'O, ,RNAM 'GREL LA YANG THUGS LHAG PAR MOS PA ZHIG YOD PAS,
DGE BSHES BZANG

PO'I RIGS DANG CHOS KYI GSUNG GLING MDZAD KABS,  RNAM 'GREL GYI
DOGS DPYOD MANG DU 'ONG BA ZHIG YOD CING,  PO TI GZHAN RNAMS SE
'BRAS DGE GSUM GYI CHOS GRA'I DRIN GYIS DGA' MO 'DUG KYANG,
RNAM 'GREL GYI DKA' BA'I

RNAMS LA DENGS NGA LA GLENG TZAM BYED MKHAN YANG DKON PA 'DUG
CES THUGS SKYO BA'I RNAM PA YANG YANG MDZAD,  'DI YANG RJE BLA
MA'I RNAM THAR DAD PA'I 'JUG NGOGS LAS,  RNAM 'GREL GYI RNAM
BSHAD RIGS MDZOD LA

GZIGS RTOG MDZAD CING,  LE'U GNYIS PA'I SKABS KYI LAM GYI RNAM
BZHAG STON PA'I SKABS LA LEGS PAR GZIGS PAS RKYEN BYAS NAS,
CHOS KYI GRAGS PA'I GZHUNG LUGS DANG RIGS PA'I SROL LA DPAG TU
MED PA'I DAD PA SHUGS

NGO MNAN PAS MIN NON PA 'KHRUNGS SHING,  STON DER BZHUGS KYI
RING LA RNAM 'GREL GYI GZHUNG LA GZIGS TZAM NAS DAD PA'I SPRUL
LONG GYOS TE SPYAN CHAB KYI RGYUN BCAD PAR MI NUS PA RTAG TU
'ONG BA ZHIG BYUNG GSUNGS SO,  ,ZHES

GSUNGS PA DANG RJES SU THUN PA NYID DO, ,CHOS GSUNG BA'I TSE
YANG RNAM 'GREL GYI RIGS PAS SGRUB TSUL RTZAL 'DON GYIS GSUNG BA
ZHIG CING,  DUS PHYIS RJE BTZUN 'JAM PA'I DBYANGS KYIS MNAL LAM
DU RNAM 'GREL LAM GYI RIM

PAR BSGRIGS PA'I LEGS BSHAD KYI SKYES KYANG STZOL BAR MDZAD
SNANG STE 'OG TU 'GOD PAR BYA'O, ,DBU TSAD KYI GZHUNG GI YANG
DAG PA'I RIGS LAM LA THUGS GTZIGS CHE BAR MDZAD PA 'DI NI SHIN
TU GNAD CHE BAR MTHONG STE,  CI'I PHYIR ZHE NA

RGYAL BA GNYIS PA CONG KHA PA CHEN POS,  SMRA BA'I KHYU MCHOG
'PHAGS PA YAB SRAS DANG, ,LOG SMRA TSAR GCOD PHYOGS GLANG GRAGS
PA LAS, ,LEGS PAR 'ONGS PA'I RIGS LAM BDUD RTZI'I CHUS, ,BLO MIG
DRI MA YANG YANG MA BRKUS NA, ,SHIN TU

ZAB GNAS MTHONG BA SMOS CI DGOS,  RIGS PA'I LUNG DON LA YANG
DPYAD PA NA, ,PHAL CHER LOG PAR RTOG PA 'PHEL 'GYUR ZHING, ,GAL
TE YANG DAG DAM BCA' TZAM ZHIG GI, ,NGES PA RNYED KYANG SGRUB
DANG SUN 'BYIN GYI, ,TSAD MA'I STOBS KYIS

063 **, ,THE TSOM MI CHOD PHYIR, ,'DAM LA BTAB PA'I PHUR PA
BZHIN 'GYUR BAS, ,YANG DAG BAG CHAGS BRTAN PO 'JOG MI NUS, ,ZHES
DANG,  DE PHYIR BLO GROS PHRA ZHING MJANGS PA DANG, ,KU SHA'I
RTZE LTAR MGYUR DE

SRID DU, ,NGOMS MI SLA BAR RIGS PA'I GZHUNG LUGS LA, ,MKHAS PA'I
BSHES LA BRTEN TE LEGS PAR SBYANGS, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA'I PHYIR RO,
,DE LTAR GZHUNG CHEN MO RNAMS LA THUGS SBYANGS MDZAD PA YANG JI
SKAD DU,  RIGS DPE CHA LAS

BSLABS SHING, ,BLA MA'I DRUNG NAS MA YIN PA, ,'PHYON MA'I BUD
MED SBRUM MA BZHIN, ,TSOGS KYI NANG NA MDZES MA YIN, ,ZHES PA'I
DPE LTA BU MA YIN PAR,  DENG SANG PO TI CHEN PO RNAMS KYI GZHUNG
BSHAD KYI RGYUN PHAL CHER NUB

'DUG NA'ANG,  GANG YOD RNAMS BSHES GNYEN MKHAS PA RNAMS LAS SNGA
PHYI CI RIGS SU ZHIB TU GSAN CING BSHAD RGYUN MED PA RNAMS LA
BKLAG LUNG GI RGYUN YAN CHAD GSAN PAR MDZAD SNANG STE ZHIB PAR
SO SO'I THAD KAR 'BRI BAR

BYA'O,         ,GANG YANG 'DI NA GZHUNG TSIG KHOL BYUNG TZAM
'GA' KHA TON BYED PA NYID LA SNGE SNOD 'DZIN PAR SMRA, ,NYUD
NGU'I THAL PHRENG BZLAS BRJOD LHUR LEN GZHAN SMOD TSIG GI NGUG
MDA' 'PHEN LA SMRA BA'I SENG GER SGROGS, ,

THOS PA'I SNANG BA DANG BRAL BLUN SGOM MUN PA'I MAL DU GYI NAR
NYAL LA GRUB PA'I DBANG PO ZER, ,MI SHES GDOL PA'I PHRU GU DAR
ZAB KYIS DRKIS MTHON PO'I STEGS LA 'KHOD NAS 'GRO BA 'DREN PAR
RLOM, ,SNYIGS MA'I NGANG TSUL 'PHYON

MA'I GAR 'DI LA, ,SNYIGS MA'I SKYE BO BLUN PO MGU SRID KYANG,
,DAM PA RNAMS KYI LAS SU BYA BA NI, ,DAM PA'I CHOS LA CHOS BZHIN
SPYOD PA YIN, ,DE NI THOS BSAM SGOM PA'I LAM ZHUGS NAS, ,DE
BZHIN GSHEGS PA'I GRONG DU BGROD PA STE, ,

DE BAS DANG POR THOS PA 'TSOL BYA ZHES, ,DE LTAR DGONGS NAS DED
DPON MKHAS PA 'DI, ,THOS BSAM GRU CHEN ZHON NAS NYIN BZHIN DU,
,GZHUNG LUGS RGYA MTSO'I KHYON KUN NYUL BA LAS, ,RNYED PAR DKA'
ZHING RNYED NA DON CHE BA'I, ,

ZAB DON NOR BU GRANGS MED 'DOD DGUR BLANGS, ,DE TSE BDEN GNYIS
SHES BYA'I DKYIL 'KHOR NI, ,NAM MKHA' BZHIN DU RGYA CHE ZHES
GRAGS KYANG, ,'DI YI MKHYEN RAB YANGS RGYA MTSO YIS, ,GZHAL
BYA'I GNAS KUN RMIG RJES CHU

BZHIN BYAS, ,TSUL DE MA BZOD GZHUNG BZANG CHU BO STONG, ,RANG
RANG RJOD DON LHUR LHUNG SGROGS BZHIN DU, ,NYIN BZHIN GANG THUGS
CHU GTER LA ZHUGS KYANG, ,DOGS PA MED PAR BZUNG PAS SKYENGS PAR
GYUR, ,'DI NA MKHAS PAR GRAGS

PA PHAL MO CHES, ,'BAD KYANG BLO YI SPYOD YUL MA GYUR BA, ,BLO
BZANG RGYAL BA'I LEGS BSHAD DKA' GNAD KUN, ,'DI YIS LAG PA'I
MTHIL GYI RDZAS BZHIN GZIGS, ,PHYOGS GLANG CHOS KYI GRAGS PA LAS
'ONGS PA'I, ,YANG DAG RIGS

TSUL GLOG GI DRA BA YANG, ,'DI YI YID 'ONG ZHAL GYI CHU 'DZIN
DBUS, ,NYAMS 'GYUR STONG PHRAG 'KHYUGS PA'I GAR RTZEN, ,MES PO'I
RNA BA BRGYAD KYIS MA THOS PA'I, ,MKHAS PA'I LEGS BSHAD MA LUS
'DI YIS DSAN, ,DBANG PO'I

064 **, ,'DRIN BYED STONG GIS MA MTHONG BA'I, ,ZAB DON DKA' GNAD
MA LUS 'DI YIS GZIGS, ,'DI LTA'I YON TAN LCAGS KYU YIS, ,BDAG
YID GNYIS 'THUNG DRANGS GYUR TE, ,CHEN PO GZHAN GYI SPYOD TSUL
LA, ,GUS PA

GTING NAS LHOD PAR GYUR, ,SHES BYA'I DKYIL 'KHOR GCIG CAR 'GENGS
PA YI, ,MKHYEN BZANG NYI MA STONG PHRAG 'BAR BA'I GZIS, ,LKOG
GYUR THUN GSUM MING GI MTHAR BKRAD PA'I, ,YE SHES SGYU 'PHRUL
ROL PAR PHYAG BGYI'O,          ,

TAR BKA' POD CHEN PO RNAMS LA THOS BSAM GTZO BOR MDZAD PA'I BAR
SKABS RNAMS SU DGE BA'I BSHES GNYEN GSUM LA ZAB PA DANG RGYA CHE
BA'I CHOS KYI RNAM GRANGS YANG MANG DU GSAN PAR MDZAD DE,  DE
YANG THOG MAR DPAL RDO RJE 'JIGS

BYED CHEN PO SOGS LHAG PA'I LHA DU MA'I ZHAL MNGON SUM DU GZIGS
SHING,  GRUB PA'I GO 'PHANG MTHON PO LA MNGA' BRNYES PA RJE
THU'U BKVAN PA NGAG DBANG CHOS KYI RGYA MTSO'I DRUNG NAS RAS
BRIS KYI DKYIL 'KHOR DU DPAL RDO RJE 'JIGS BYED LHA

BCU GSUM MA'I DBANG BZHI YONGS SU RDZOGS PA STA GON DANG BCAS PA
BRGYUD PA'I CHU BO GSUM 'DRES KYI GDAMS PAS BRGYAN PA'I SMIN
BYED KYI RIM PA RGYAS PAR GSAN,  SKU TSE 'DI LA DBANG CHEN GSAN
PA'I THOG MA 'DI YIN 'DUG PAS,

DUS PHYIS PHRAN LA KHED RANG GI SKYE BA GONG MA DE NYID NGOS CAG
SNGAGS KYI SGOR THOG MAR 'JUG MKHAN GYI RDO RJE SLOB DPON YIN
PAS BKA' DRIN SHIN TU ZHES YANG YANG GSUNG,  RJE THU'U BKVAN RIN
PO CHES SNGA MO LCANG SKYA GONG MA RJE NGAG DBANG BLO

BZANG CHOS LDAN PA'I DRUNG NAS 'JIGS BYED KYI DBANG GSAN PA'I
NUB MO RMI LAM DU,  GZHAL YAS KHANG RNGAM BRJID CHE BA ZHIG GI
DBUS NA,  ZA 'OG 'BOL MANG PO BRTZEGS PA'I KHRI MTHON PO ZHIG
KHAR RDO RJE 'CHANG LCANG SKYA PA BZHUGS

PA'I PHYOGS GCIG TU DE 'DRA'I KHRI GZHAN 'DUG PA LA RANG NYID
BKOD NAS,  BLA MA GRI GUG DAR TSON SNA LNGAS MTSAN PA ZHIG GTAD
DE,  'DI RE ZHIG KHYED RANG GIS TSAGS GYIS,  SLAR YANG DED LA
'PHROD PA BYED DGOS SO ZHES GSUNGS PA

ZHIG RMIS PA DA RES SPRUL SKU RIN PO CHER RDO RJE 'JIGS BYED GYI

DPON SLOB THUN MONG NAS TSOGS 'KHOR RGAS PA ZHIG MDZAD PAR,
TSOGS RJAS KYI NANG MCHOD KHOL ZHING

'PHYUR BA DANG,  GNAS 'ONGS CHA MED PA'I SHING THOG AA RU RA'I

'BRONG RTZE LHA BRTZUN RIN PO CHEN RGYA MTSOS MDZAD PA'I

RGYAL MTSAN GYI LAM RIM TSIGS BCAD MA,  BLO SBYONG DON BDUN MA
DANG,  TSIGS BRGYAD MA,  BZANG SPYOD DANG SMON LAM BDUN CU PA
RNAMS CHAG MED DU ZHAL 'DON MDZAD CING DON LA BSHAR SGOM MDZAD
PA YIN GSUNGS,  'DI NI 'BROM

RIN PO CHES,  RJE SANGS RGYAS BYA BA KUN MKHYEN YIN, ,DE SPANGS
RTOGS TSOGS GNYIS MTHAR PHYIN YIN, ,NGA PHA MA'I DON DU DE 'DOD
PAS, ,DUS DANG POR THOS PAS SGRO 'DOGS BCAD, ,DUS GNYIS PAR BSAM
PAS SGRO 'DOGS BCAD,,

DUS GSUM PAR BSGOM PAS SGRO 'DOGS BCAD, ,KYE DE YANG GCIGG NYID
MA YIN TE, ,NGA THOS DUS TSE NA BSAM BSGOM BDO, ,NGA BSAM DUS
TSE NA THOS BSGOM BDO, ,NGA BSGOM DUS TSE NA THOS BSAM BDO, ,NGA
GCIG TU MA LUS BSDOMS

BYAS NAS, ,CHOS LAM DU KHYER NAS SHES PAS, ,NGA BKA' GDAMS
PHYOGS CHAR MA LHUNG BAS, ,DON RGYA 'BAG BZHIN DU 'PHUL SHES
PA'I, ,LEGS KUN TU RTOGS TE BKA' GDAMS YIN, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA
DANG,  RJE BLA MA RNAG GIS

KYANG,  DE LTAR THOS BSAM GNAD DU LEGS SONG NA, ,DE NYID BSGOM
DANG LEN GTZO BO YIN, ,THOS BSAM SGOM GSUM CIG CAR 'BYUNG BAS
NA, ,TSEGS MED LAM GYI RTOGS PA RNYED PAR 'GYUR, ,RGYA BOD MKHAS
PA'I SKYE BO PHAL

MO CHES, ,MTSAMS DANG 'DAG SPYAR GCIG DRIL MDZAD KYANG, ,'CHAD
RTZOD RTZOM PA'I MDZAD PA MDZAD BZHIN PAR, ,SA LAM RTOGS PA PHUL
BYUNG RNYED LA LTOS, ,ZHES GSUNGS PA LTAR,  THOS BSAM SGOM GSUM
YA BRAL DU MA GYUR BAR GCIG

GCIG GI GROGS SU 'KHYER SHES PA JO BO BKA' GDAMS PA'I RNAM PAR
THAR PA PHYAG LEN DU BTAB PA'I RNAM RMAD DU BYUNG BA'O, ,MKHAS
PA'I BYA BA 'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM GSUM KYANG DGUNG LO SHIN TU PRA
BA'I GNAS SKABS 'DI RANG NAS BDAG

GIR BZHES PA YIN TE,  DGUNG LO BCU GCIG PA'I DUS SU DAD LDAN GYI
GRA SLOB SPYIN BDAG MANG PO ZHIG GIS GSOL BA BTAB PAS,  SKYABS
'GRO'I KHRID KYI BKA' 'CHOS DANG,  LAM GYI GTZO BO RNAM GSUM GYI
BSHAD PA SHIN TU RNO BA ZHIG MDZAD PAS,

THAMS CAD KYI YID RANG DBANG MED PAR 'PHROG STE DAD PA'I SHUGS
KYIS MIG NAS MCHI MA RANG DBANG MED PAR 'CHOR BA BYUNG,  DE NAS
BZUNG ZHU BA PO RNAMS KYI MOS PA BZHIN DBANG CHEN GYI RIGS MA
GTOGS GSUNG CHOS GANG ZHUS THAMS CAD

THOGS PA MED PAR GNANG NAS THAMS CAD YID TSIM PAR MDZAD,  RTZOD
PA YANG DGUNG LO BCU BDUN GYI SKABS GZHUNG LUGS LA SBYANGS PA'I
SPOBS PA MCHOG TU DGE BA AU CU MU CHIN GU SHR'AI BZONG PA ZHES
BYA BAS NYAM SAD KYI TSUL DU RTZA SHES KYI

RAB BYED DANG PO'I SHO LO KA KHA SHAS LAS BRTZAMS PA'I DA YID

BSGRIGS TE LUNG RIGS DRI MA MED PA'I LAM LAS DRANGS PA'I RTZO DA
LAN GNANG,  DE LA DAG BZHAG GI

071 **, ,TSUL GYIS RTZOD YIG YANG SKYAR PHUL BA LA,  SLAR YANG

'BUM DU BZHUGS PA LTAR YIN NO, ,PHYI AU GU SHR'A'IDE SKU MDUN DU

DU BZHUGS,  ?GONG MA'I GSOL THAB RANG NAS GSOL CHAS NAR MA DANG,

GUR SOGS NYE BAR MKHO BA'I YO BYAD THAMS CAD GNANG ZHING,  PHYAG
GYOG PA RNAMS

NAS CHOS BKA' RNAM GRANGS DU MA ZHIG

TU PHEBS PA NA,  TI SHRI'A CHEN PO'I LUNG LAS KYI MNGON PAR MTHO
BA GNANG RGYU YIN TSUL GYI

BKA' BZANG PO PHEBS SO,         ,SA LA GNAS PA'I SEMS DPA'
CHEN PO ZHIG  ,SA CHEN SKYONG BA'I RGYAL PO'I TSUL BZUNG BA,
,SA YI TSANGS PA GONG MA YUNG tING ZHES,  ,SA GSUM GRAGS PA'I BA
DAN GYO BA DES, ,

GSER LDAN LJONGS 'DI'I GZHAN GYIS RNYID DKA' BA'I,  ,GSER BZANG
THAM KA GZI 'OD 'BAR BA DANG,  ,GSER YIG 'JA' SA PHUL NAS RNAM
'DREN KHYOD, ,GSER GYI LUNG GIS CHAB SRID BLA MAR BSNGAGS,
,'DZAM GLING MKHAS

PA'I GTZUG RGYAN 'GRO BA'I MGON,  ,'DZAM GLING SKYONG BA'I RGYAL
POS BKUR BA'I GTAM,  ,'DZAM BU'I GLING 'DI'I SKYE RGU'I RNA BA
LA,  ,'DZAM BU'I GSER GYI RGYAN BZHIN MDZES PAR GYUR,  ,GANG GI
STOBS 'BYOR ZHAGS PAS NOR

'DZIN KHYON,  ,CIG CAR 'CHING BA GNAM BSKOS MI RJES,  ,BSTI
STANG BGYID NA DREGS LDAN GZHAN DAG GIS,  , ZHABS LA SPYI POS MI
'DUD RANG DBANG CI,  ,'PHRIN LAS BCU GNYIS BDAG PO'I SNANG BA
YIS,  ,THUB BSTAN PAD MA'I DGA'

TSAL BZHAD PA LAS,  ,PHAN BDE SPRANG RTZIS LUS CAN SKANG DRUG
TSOGS,  ,TSIM MDZAD BSTAN 'GRO'I MGON LA BDAG PHYAG 'TSAL,
,ZHES BYA BA NI BAR SKABS KYI TSIGS SU BCAD PA'O,  , KHYAB BDAG
RDO RJE SEMS DPA'I NGO BO DPAL LDAN BLA MA

DAM PA YE SHES BSTAN PA'I SGRON ME DPAL BZANG PO'I RNAM PAR THAR

PHRA MO'I GNAS SKABS NYID NAS MKHAS GRUB CHEN PO'I THAR BDAG GIR
MDZAD CING,  'JAM DBYANGS

?GONG MA CHEN POS T'A KOO SHR'AI'I LUNG LAS PHUL TE CHAB SRID
CHEN PO'I BLA MAR BKUR BA'I LE'U STE LNGA PA'O,,         ,,DE
NAS RJE BLA MA MCHOG GI THUGS DGONGS LA,  ,BOD DBUS GTZANG CHOS
KYI ZHING KHAMS SU PHEBS THUB PA ZHIG BYUNG NA

DON SHIN TU CHE BAR GZIGS NAS,  PHEBS 'DUN GYI DGONGS PA RGYUN
LDAN DU MDZAD KYANG ?GONG MA CHEN POR GNAS TSUL ZHU MA BDE BAS,
RJE SEMS DPA' CHEN PO THU'U BKVAN RIN PO CHER DE DON LA GSUNG
BRTAG ZHU BA GNANG BAR,  LAN CHAGS

GTOR MA 'BUM THER BTANG NA BZHED DON 'GRUB CES PHEBS,  RJE RANG

DANG CHES GOS GSOL BA ZHIG DMIGS BRTZEM 'BUM THER DANG,  LAN
CHAGS GTOR MA MANG DU BTANG NA THUGS

083**, ,BZHED BDE BLAG TU 'GRUB CES GSUNGS PA CIG RMIS PAS RIM
GRO RNAMS BSGRUB PA MDZAD CING,  KHYAD PAR DU DMIGS BRTZE MA
DANG,  DGE LEGS YON TAN MA DANG BLO BZANG RGYAL PA MA SHO LO KA BCAS
 
SO SO NAS 'BUM THER RE ZHAL 'DON GNANG BAS,  NUB GCIG PAn CHEN
BLO BZANG YE SHES YIN ZER BA'I BLA MA ZHIG DANG MJAL BA RMIS,
PHYIS SU BOD DU PHEBS NAS PAn CHEN DANG MJAL BAS,  ZHAL NYAMS
DANG SKU'I DBYIBS SOGS THUGS RMIS

SU BYUNG BA DE KHO NA LTA BU 'DUG CES GSUNGS,  DE NAS RING PO MA
LON PAR ?GONG MA CHEN POS RJE 'DI NYID LA ?RGYAL DBANG THAMS CAD
MKHYEN PA MGAR THAR NAS BOD DU GDAN 'DREN PA'I MI SNAR PHEBS
NAS,  DBUS GTZANG CHOS KYI ZHING DU

RGYAL BA YAB SRAS KYI DRUNG BKA' CHOS GSAN PAR YUN MI THUNG TZAM
BZHUGS CHOG PA'I BKA' BZANG PO PHEBS PAR,  RING MO ZHIG GNAS
THUGS LA BRNAG PA'I DON KHYAD PAR CAN DE DA 'GRUB PAR 'DUG SNYAM
PA'I DGYES TSOR BSAM GYIS

MI KHYAB PA BYUNG SNANG NGO,          ,RGYAL BA KUN GYI YE SHES
GCIG BSDUS PA, ,'JAM PA'I DBYANGS TE DE NYID DUR SMRIG GI, ,RNAM
ROL BDAG GI BLA MA DE YI THUGS, ,RTAG TU CHOS KYI BDUD RTZI LA
CHAGS PAS,  ,BKA' BSTAN

MDO SNGAGS CHES KYI NYAL 'GRO KUN, ,GCIG TU 'KHYIL BA'I GNAS NI

SKAR 'OD KYIS RTZEN PA BZHIN, ,LJONGS

DER JO SH'AKA RNAM GNYIS GTZO GYUR PA'I, ,NGO MTSAR RTEN MANG

'KHOR LO'I MTSAN BZANG GIS, ,SA

084**, ,KHAB CHEN PO NAS CHIBS BSKYOD GNAD BA LA,  THU'U BKVAN

GSUNGS PA DE KHO NA BZHIN BYUNG 'DUG  ,DE NAS RIM GYIS PHEBS PAS
MGAR THAR NAS

?GONG THAMS CAD MKHYEN PAS MGRON GNYER NANG SO BLO BZANG DKON

DANG,  DE RJES LHA SRAS,  MCHOG SPRUL RIN PO CHE,  AM BAN NE GE

BRJOD MDZAD PAS,  NUB PHYOGS KYI BHA GA'I DBYIBS CAN GYI BRAG GI
BU NAS BLO BUR DU CHU RDOL BA THAMS CAD

ZHAL MDZUM PA MDZAD PA LAS MING DNGOS SU MA GNANG,        SPRUL
PA'I GNAS MCHOG DPAL GYI RVA

SGRENG DU,  ,SPRUL PA'I SKYES MCHOG DU LHAN CIG 'DZOM,  , SPRUL

'GRO MA,  ,GSANG BA YE SHES

BDO'I GNAS SKABS 'DIR,  ,GZHI TSUL KHRIMS RNAM DAG SNA GCIG
KYANG,  ,BSRUNG NUS PHAN YON DPAG MED 'THOB,  ,DON DE SDOM GSUM
BCAS MCHAMS RNAMS,  ,SROG BSDOS TE BSRUNG BA GNAD DU CHE,  ,CHOS
GZHUNG LUGS BRGYA PHRAG

THOS GYUR KYANG,  ,KHA PHYIR LTA'I 'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM PA LA,  YID
GYENGS PAS NYAMS SU MA BLANGS NA,  ,DGRA GSHIN RJE'I PHO NYAS
ZIN PA'I TSE,  ,SEMS 'GYOD PAS GDUNG BA'I RGYU RU ZAD,  ,'KHOR
GNYEN BSHES BU SLOB  SKYONG RNAMS,  ,

DGRA NYON MONGS DPUNG TSOGS RGYAS PA'I RGYU,  ,LAS DANG PO PA
YIS SPANGS NA LEGS,  ,GROGS BYA DANG RI DVAGS BAG PHEBS RGYU,
,CHU KLUNG RGYUN LHUNG LHUNG DAL GYIS SGROG  ,GNAS RTZI SHING
NAGS TSAL MDZES PAS BRGYAN,  ,YID CHAGS SDAD

SKYE BA'I RGYU DANG BRAL,  ,GNAS DE 'DRA DAM CHOS 'PHEL BA'I
RGYU, ,DE BSTEN PAR MDZOD CIG SKAL LDAN DAG  ,SNGON BYON PA'I
MKHA GRUB BGRANG YAS KYIS,  ,CHOS ZAB DGU MANG DU GSUNGS LAGS
KYANG,  ,RJE THUB PA'I DBANG PO'I GSUNG RAB KUN,,

DON MTSANG MED PAR GCIG BSDUS PA,  ,BLO MCHOG DMAN KUN LA PHAN
PA'I CHOS,  ,LTA SGOM DANG SPYOD PA MA 'KHRUL BA,  ,KHONG BLO
BZANG GRAGS PA'I LEGS PAR BSHAD,  ,GZHUNG BYANG CHUB LAM RIM LAS
GZHAN GANG,  ,DE NYAMS LEN MDZOD CIG

SKAL LDAN DAG  ,SNGON THOG MED DUS NAS BSAGS PA YI,  ,LAS NYON
MONGS SGRIB PA CHES 'THUG PAS,  ,LAM RTOGS PA SKYE BA'I GEGS
MANG YANG,  ,ZHING MCHOG GYUR BLA MA DKON MCHOG LA,  ,YID GDUNG
SHUGS DRAG POS GSOL BTAB NAS,  ,TSOGS  

GSOG DANG SGRIB SBYONG LA 'BAD NA,  ,LAM RTOGS PA BDE BLAG SKYE
BA LAGS,  ,TSUL DE LA 'BUNGS CIG SKAL LDAN DAG  ,CHOS DGE SBYOR
GANG DANG GANG BYED KYANG,  ,THABS BYANG CHUB SEMS KYIS ZIN PA
DANG,  ,MJUG BYANG CHUB 'THOB PHYIR RAB BSNGOS NA, ,

LAM THEG PA CHEN POR 'GYUR LAGS PAS,  ,DE GNAD DU ZUNGS SHIG
SKAL LDAN DAG  ,MCHOG SANGS RGYAS 'THOB PA'I LAM GYI GNAD,  ,LUS
YONGS SU RDZOGS PAR NYIN RE BZHIN,  ,BSHAR SGOM GYIS NYAMS SU
BLANGS BYAS TE,  ,LAM ZAB MOR BAG

CHAGS 'JOG PA DANG,  ,SKABS GANG BBAS DMIGS PAR GCIG DRIL BA,
,YID CHOS LA RTAG TU 'DRIS PA DANG,  LAM PHYOGS RENG MI 'GRO'I
GNAD CIG GDA',  ,DE SNYING GTAM YIN NO SKAL LDAN DAG  ,RGYUD
RNAM PAR DAG PA LAS GSUNGS PA'I,  ,
